# Mobile file sharing tsx

import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { mobileStyles } from './mobileStyles';
import { API_BASE, formatFileSize, getTimeRemaining, retryOperation, UploadedFile, DownloadProgress, UploadProgress } from './types';
import JSZip from 'jszip';

interface MobileFileSharingProps {
  sessionId: string;
  handleLogout: () => void;
}

export function MobileFileSharing({ sessionId, handleLogout }: MobileFileSharingProps) {
  const [uploadedFiles, setUploadedFiles] = useState<UploadedFile[]>([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [downloadProgress, setDownloadProgress] = useState<DownloadProgress | null>(null);
  const [uploadProgress, setUploadProgress] = useState<UploadProgress | null>(null);
  const [defaultExpirationMinutes, setDefaultExpirationMinutes] = useState(5);
  const [filesCurrentlyUploading, setFilesCurrentlyUploading] = useState<File[] | null>(null);
  const xhrRef = useRef<XMLHttpRequest | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchUserSettings = async () => {
      if (!sessionId) return;
      
      try {
        const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/settings`, {
          headers: {
            'sessionid': sessionId
          }
        });
        
        if (res.ok) {
          const data = await res.json();
          if (data.defaultExpirationMinutes) {
            setDefaultExpirationMinutes(data.defaultExpirationMinutes);
            localStorage.setItem('defaultExpirationMinutes', data.defaultExpirationMinutes.toString());
          }
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching user settings:', error);
      }
    };

    fetchUserSettings();
  }, [sessionId]);

  useEffect(() => {
    window.scrollTo(0, 0);
  }, []);

  const handleFileChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    if (e.target.files) {
      const newFiles = Array.from(e.target.files);
      handleFileUpload(newFiles);
      e.target.value = '';
    }
  };

  const handleFileUpload = async (filesToUpload: File[]) => {
    if (filesToUpload.length === 0) return;
    
    setIsLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    setFilesCurrentlyUploading(filesToUpload);
    
    try {
      const formData = new FormData();
      const totalSize = filesToUpload.reduce((acc, file) => acc + file.size, 0);
      
      filesToUpload.forEach(file => {
        formData.append('files', file);
      });
      
      setUploadProgress({
        fileName: filesToUpload.length === 1 ? filesToUpload[0].name : `${filesToUpload.length} files`,
        progress: 0,
        totalSize
      });
      
      const uploadOperation = async () => {
        const xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
        xhrRef.current = xhr;
        
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          xhr.upload.addEventListener('progress', (event) => {
            if (event.lengthComputable) {
              const progress = (event.loaded / event.total) * 100;
              setUploadProgress(prev => prev ? {
                ...prev,
                progress
              } : null);
            }
          });

          xhr.addEventListener('load', () => {
            xhrRef.current = null;
            if (xhr.status >= 200 && xhr.status < 300) {
              try {
                resolve(JSON.parse(xhr.responseText));
              } catch (e) {
                reject(new Error('Invalid response from server'));
              }
            } else {
              reject(new Error(`Upload failed with status ${xhr.status}`));
            }
          });

          xhr.addEventListener('error', () => {
            xhrRef.current = null;
            reject(new Error('Network error occurred during upload'));
          });
          
          xhr.addEventListener('abort', () => {
            xhrRef.current = null;
            console.log('Upload aborted by user.');
          });

          xhr.open('POST', `${API_BASE}/upload`);
          xhr.setRequestHeader('sessionid', sessionId);
          xhr.setRequestHeader('expirationminutes', defaultExpirationMinutes.toString());
          xhr.withCredentials = true;
          xhr.send(formData);
        });
      };
      
      await retryOperation(uploadOperation);
      await fetchFiles();
      
    } catch (err: any) {
      if (err.name !== 'AbortError') {
        console.error('Upload error:', err);
        setError(err.message || 'Failed to upload files');
      }
    } finally {
      if (xhrRef.current !== null) {
          setIsLoading(false);
          setUploadProgress(null);
          setFilesCurrentlyUploading(null);
          xhrRef.current = null;
      }
    }
  };

  const handleCancelUpload = () => {
    if (xhrRef.current) {
      xhrRef.current.abort();
      setIsLoading(false);
      setUploadProgress(null);
      setFilesCurrentlyUploading(null);
      setError('Upload cancelled.');
      setTimeout(() => setError(null), 3000);
      xhrRef.current = null;
    }
  };

  const fetchFiles = async () => {
    if (!sessionId) return;
    
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/files`, {
        headers: { 'sessionid': sessionId },
        credentials: 'include'
      });
      
      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error('Failed to fetch files');
      }
      
      const data = await response.json();
      const now = Date.now();
      const activeFiles = data.filter(file => file.expiresAt > now);
      setUploadedFiles(activeFiles);
      
    } catch (err: any) {
      setError(err.message);
      if (err.message.includes('Unauthorized')) {
        handleLogout();
      }
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    if (sessionId) {
      fetchFiles();
    }
  }, [sessionId]);

  const activeFiles = uploadedFiles.filter(file => file.expiresAt > Date.now());
  const uploadingTotalSize = filesCurrentlyUploading?.reduce((acc, file) => acc + file.size, 0) ?? 0;

  return (
    <>
      <div style={mobileStyles.mobileCard}>
        <div style={mobileStyles.mobileContent}>
          <div style={{ flexShrink: 0 }}>
            <div style={mobileStyles.mobileUploadSection}>
              <input 
                type="file"
                multiple 
                onChange={handleFileChange}
                id="mobile-file-input"
                style={{ display: 'none' }}
              />

              <div style={{...mobileStyles.mobileUploadArea, margin: '0 16px'}} onClick={() => document.getElementById('mobile-file-input')?.click()}>
                <svg width="40" height="40" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style={{opacity: 0.8}}>
                  <path d="M12 16L12 8" stroke="#333" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                  <path d="M9 11L12 8 15 11" stroke="#333" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                  <path d="M20 16.7428C21.2215 15.734 22 14.2079 22 12.5C22 9.46243 19.5376 7 16.5 7C16.2815 7 16.0771 6.886 15.9661 6.69774C14.6621 4.48484 12.2544 3 9.5 3C5.35786 3 2 6.35786 2 10.5C2 12.5661 2.83545 14.4371 4.18695 15.7935" stroke="#333" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                </svg>
                <div style={{ marginTop: '16px', textAlign: 'center' }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: '17px', fontWeight: '500', marginBottom: '8px' }}>
                    Upload Files
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: '15px', color: '#666' }}>
                    Tap to choose files
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              {filesCurrentlyUploading && isLoading && (
                <div style={{ 
                  padding: '16px', 
                  border: '1px solid #e0e0e0', 
                  borderRadius: '12px', 
                  backgroundColor: '#f8f8f8', 
                  margin: '20px 16px',
                  boxShadow: '0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.05)'
                }}>
                  <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: '12px' }}>
                    <h3 style={{ margin: 0, fontSize: '15px', fontWeight: '500' }}>
                      Uploading ({filesCurrentlyUploading.length} file{filesCurrentlyUploading.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''} - {formatFileSize(uploadingTotalSize)})
                    </h3>
                    <button
                      onClick={handleCancelUpload}
                      style={{
                        background: 'none',
                        border: '1px solid #ffcdd2',
                        padding: '6px 12px',
                        borderRadius: '8px',
                        fontSize: '13px',
                        color: '#e53935',
                        fontWeight: '500'
                      }}
                    >
                      Cancel
                    </button>
                  </div>
                  <ul style={{ listStyle: 'none', padding: 0, margin: 0, maxHeight: '120px', overflowY: 'auto' }}>
                    {filesCurrentlyUploading.map((file, index) => (
                      <li key={`${file.name}-${index}`} style={{ 
                        display: 'flex', 
                        justifyContent: 'space-between', 
                        alignItems: 'center', 
                        fontSize: '14px', 
                        padding: '8px 0', 
                        borderBottom: index === filesCurrentlyUploading.length - 1 ? 'none' : '1px solid #eee' 
                      }}>
                        <span style={{ 
                          overflow: 'hidden', 
                          textOverflow: 'ellipsis', 
                          whiteSpace: 'nowrap', 
                          marginRight: '10px', 
                          flex: 1 
                        }}>
                          {file.name}
                        </span>
                        <span style={{ color: '#666', whiteSpace: 'nowrap' }}>{formatFileSize(file.size)}</span>
                      </li>
                    ))}
                  </ul>
                  {uploadProgress && (
                     <div style={{ marginTop: '14px' }}>
                       <div style={{ height: '6px', backgroundColor: '#e0e0e0', borderRadius: '3px', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
                         <div 
                           style={{
                             height: '100%',
                             width: `${uploadProgress.progress}%`,
                             backgroundColor: '#4CAF50',
                             transition: 'width 0.2s ease',
                           }}
                         />
                       </div>
                       <div style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: '#666', marginTop: '6px', textAlign: 'right' }}>
                         {Math.round(uploadProgress.progress)}%
                       </div>
                     </div>
                   )}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>

          <div style={mobileStyles.mobileSection}>
            <div style={{ 
              display: 'flex', 
              justifyContent: 'space-between', 
              alignItems: 'center',
              marginBottom: '16px'
            }}>
              <h2 style={mobileStyles.mobileSectionTitle}>Your Files</h2>
              {activeFiles.length > 0 && (
                <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px' }}>
                  <button
                    style={{
                      background: 'none',
                      border: '1px solid #e0e0e0',
                      padding: '8px 14px',
                      borderRadius: '8px',
                      fontSize: '14px',
                      display: 'flex',
                      alignItems: 'center',
                      gap: '6px',
                      color: '#333',
                      fontWeight: '500'
                    }}
                    onClick={async () => {
                      try {
                        const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-');
                        const folderName = `sendi-files-${timestamp}`;
                        
                        const zip = new JSZip();
                        const folder = zip.folder(folderName);
                        
                        if (!folder) {
                          throw new Error('Failed to create zip folder');
                        }

                        setDownloadProgress({
                          fileId: 'all',
                          progress: 0,
                          fileName: 'Preparing files...'
                        });

                        let completedFiles = 0;
                        for (const file of activeFiles) {
                          try {
                            setDownloadProgress({
                              fileId: 'all',
                              progress: (completedFiles / activeFiles.length) * 100,
                              fileName: `Downloading ${file.originalName}`
                            });

                            const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/download/${file.id}`, {
                              headers: {
                                'sessionid': sessionId
                              },
                              credentials: 'include'
                            });

                            if (!response.ok) {
                              console.error(`Failed to download file ${file.originalName}`);
                              continue;
                            }

                            const blob = await response.blob();
                            folder.file(file.originalName, blob);
                            completedFiles++;
                          } catch (error) {
                            console.error(`Error downloading file ${file.originalName}:`, error);
                          }
                        }

                        setDownloadProgress({
                          fileId: 'all',
                          progress: 95,
                          fileName: 'Creating zip file...'
                        });

                        const content = await zip.generateAsync({ type: 'blob' });
                        const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(content);
                        const a = document.createElement('a');
                        a.style.display = 'none';
                        a.href = url;
                        a.download = `${folderName}.zip`;
                        document.body.appendChild(a);
                        a.click();
                        window.URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
                        document.body.removeChild(a);

                        setDownloadProgress({
                          fileId: 'all',
                          progress: 100,
                          fileName: 'Download complete!'
                        });

                        setTimeout(() => {
                          setDownloadProgress(null);
                        }, 2000);

                      } catch (error) {
                        console.error('Error downloading files:', error);
                        alert('Failed to download files. Please try again.');
                        setDownloadProgress(null);
                      }
                    }}
                  >
                    <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
                      <path d="M12 16L12 8" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                      <path d="M15 13L12 16 9 13" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                      <path d="M3 15V19C3 20.1046 3.89543 21 5 21H19C20.1046 21 21 20.1046 21 19V15" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                    </svg>
                    All
                  </button>
                  <button
                    style={{
                      background: 'none',
                      border: '1px solid #ffcdd2',
                      padding: '8px 14px',
                      borderRadius: '8px',
                      fontSize: '14px',
                      display: 'flex',
                      alignItems: 'center',
                      gap: '6px',
                      color: '#e53935',
                      fontWeight: '500'
                    }}
                    onClick={async () => {
                      if (window.confirm('Are you sure you want to delete all files? This action cannot be undone.')) {
                        try {
                          const deletePromises = activeFiles.map(file =>
                            fetch(`${API_BASE}/files/${file.id}`, {
                              method: 'DELETE',
                              headers: {
                                'sessionid': sessionId
                              },
                              credentials: 'include'
                            })
                          );

                          await Promise.all(deletePromises);
                          setUploadedFiles([]);
                        } catch (error) {
                          console.error('Error deleting files:', error);
                          alert('Failed to delete all files. Please try again.');
                        }
                      }
                    }}
                  >
                    <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
                      <path d="M4 7H20" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                      <path d="M10 11V17" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                      <path d="M14 11V17" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                      <path d="M5 7L6 19C6 20.1046 6.89543 21 8 21H16C17.1046 21 18 20.1046 18 19L19 7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                      <path d="M9 7V4C9 3.44772 9.44772 3 10 3H14C14.5523 3 15 3.44772 15 4V7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                    </svg>
                    All
                  </button>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
            {activeFiles.length === 0 ? (
              <div style={mobileStyles.mobileEmptyState}>
                <div style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: '15px' }}>No files uploaded yet</div>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div style={mobileStyles.mobileFileList}>
                {activeFiles
                  .sort((a, b) => b.expiresAt - a.expiresAt)
                  .map((file) => (
                  <div key={file.id} style={{
                    padding: '16px 0',
                    borderBottom: '1px solid #eee',
                    display: 'flex',
                    flexDirection: 'column',
                    gap: '8px'
                  }} className="mobile-file-item">
                    <div style={{
                      fontSize: '15px',
                      fontWeight: '500',
                      color: '#333',
                      overflow: 'hidden',
                      textOverflow: 'ellipsis',
                      whiteSpace: 'nowrap',
                      maxWidth: '100%',
                      display: 'block',
                      cursor: 'pointer'
                    }}
                    onClick={async () => {
                      try {
                        const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/download/${file.id}`, {
                          headers: {
                            'sessionid': sessionId
                          },
                          credentials: 'include'
                        });
                        
                        if (!response.ok) {
                          if (response.status === 401) {
                            alert('Your session has expired. Please log in again.');
                            handleLogout();
                            return;
                          }
                          throw new Error(`Failed to download file: ${response.statusText}`);
                        }

                        const blob = await response.blob();
                        const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
                        const a = document.createElement('a');
                        a.style.display = 'none';
                        a.href = url;
                        a.download = file.originalName;
                        document.body.appendChild(a);
                        a.click();
                        window.URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
                        document.body.removeChild(a);
                      } catch (error) {
                        console.error('Error downloading file:', error);
                        alert('Failed to download file. Please try again.');
                      }
                    }}>
                      {file.originalName}
                    </div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: '13px', color: '#666' }}>
                      {formatFileSize(file.size)} • {getTimeRemaining(file.expiresAt)}
                    </div>
                    <div style={{ 
                      display: 'flex', 
                      gap: '10px', 
                      marginTop: '6px'
                    }}>
                      <button
                        style={{
                          ...mobileStyles.mobileFileActionButton,
                          border: '1px solid #e0e0e0',
                          backgroundColor: '#f5f5f5',
                          color: '#333'
                        }}
                        onClick={() => {
                          const url = window.location.origin + `/api/download/${file.id}`;
                          navigator.clipboard.writeText(url);
                          alert('Link copied!');
                        }}
                      >
                        <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
                          <path d="M8 5H6C4.89543 5 4 5.89543 4 7V19C4 20.1046 4.89543 21 6 21H16C17.1046 21 18 20.1046 18 19V17" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                          <path d="M20 9H10C8.89543 9 8 8.10457 8 7V3C8 1.89543 8.89543 1 10 1H16L20 5V7C20 8.10457 19.1046 9 18 9Z" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                        </svg>
                        Copy Link
                      </button>
                      <button
                        style={{
                          ...mobileStyles.mobileFileActionButton,
                          border: '1px solid #ffcdd2',
                          backgroundColor: '#fff',
                          color: '#e53935'
                        }}
                        onClick={async () => {
                          if (window.confirm('Delete this file?')) {
                            try {
                              const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/files/${file.id}`, {
                                method: 'DELETE',
                                headers: { 'sessionid': sessionId },
                                credentials: 'include'
                              });
                              
                              if (!response.ok) {
                                if (response.status === 401) {
                                  handleLogout();
                                  return;
                                }
                                throw new Error('Failed to delete file');
                              }
                              
                              setUploadedFiles(files => files.filter(f => f.id !== file.id));
                            } catch (error) {
                              console.error('Error deleting file:', error);
                              alert('Failed to delete file');
                            }
                          }
                        }}
                      >
                        <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
                          <path d="M4 7H20" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                          <path d="M10 11V17" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                          <path d="M14 11V17" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                          <path d="M5 7L6 19C6 20.1046 6.89543 21 8 21H16C17.1046 21 18 20.1046 18 19L19 7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                          <path d="M9 7V4C9 3.44772 9.44772 3 10 3H14C14.5523 3 15 3.44772 15 4V7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                        </svg>
                        Delete
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </>
  );
}

# Vulnerabilities

Let me examine the project structure first to get a better understanding of the codebase.

Ran tool
Let's first check the README.md to get an overview of the project:

Read file: README.md
Now let's examine the STRUCTURE.md file to understand the architecture better:

Read file: STRUCTURE.md
Now, let's check the server.js file to understand the server-side implementation:

Read file: server.js
Let's continue reading the important parts of server.js:

Read file: server.js
Let's check the nginx.conf file to understand the deployment setup:

Read file: nginx.conf
Let's check the package.json file to understand the dependencies:

Read file: package.json
Let's also check the sendi.service file to understand how the application is deployed:

Read file: sendi.service

Search files...
Let's check the PROBLEM_LOG.txt file to see if there are any identified issues:

Read file: PROBLEM_LOG.txt
Based on my review of the codebase, I've identified several security vulnerabilities that should be addressed. Here's a comprehensive list of security issues along with potential solutions:

## 1. Plain Text Password Storage

**Issue**: Passwords are stored in plain text in the data/users.json file.

**Solution**: Implement password hashing with a strong algorithm like bcrypt or Argon2. Add salt to each password for additional security.
```javascript
// Example implementation:
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const saltRounds = 12;

// For signup:
const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, saltRounds);
users.set(username, hashedPassword);

// For login:
const isMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, users.get(username));
if (!isMatch) return res.json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' });
```

## 2. Insecure Session Management

**Issue**: Sessions are stored in a simple Map and persisted to a JSON file with no expiration mechanism.

**Solution**: 
- Implement proper session expiration and rotation
- Use a more secure session store (like Redis)
- Add CSRF protection with tokens
```javascript
// Add expiration to sessions
const sessionData = {
  username: username,
  expiresAt: Date.now() + (24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) // 24 hours
};
sessions.set(sessionId, sessionData);

// Update authentication middleware
if (!sessionId || !sessions.has(sessionId) || sessions.get(sessionId).expiresAt < Date.now()) {
  return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
}
```

## 3. Directory Traversal Vulnerability

**Issue**: The file download functionality might be vulnerable to path traversal attacks if file paths are not properly validated.

**Solution**: 
- Validate and sanitize file paths
- Use path.resolve() to ensure files are within the uploads directory
```javascript
const filePath = path.resolve('uploads', path.basename(file.path));
if (!filePath.startsWith(path.resolve('uploads'))) {
  return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
}
```

## 4. Missing Input Validation

**Issue**: Limited validation on user inputs for file uploads, registration, and other operations.

**Solution**: Implement comprehensive input validation for all user-provided data using a library like Joi or express-validator.
```javascript
// Example with express-validator
const { body, validationResult } = require('express-validator');

app.post('/signup', [
  body('username').isAlphanumeric().isLength({ min: 4, max: 20 }),
  body('password').isLength({ min: 8 }).matches(/^(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[0-9])(?=.*[!@#$%^&*])/),
], (req, res) => {
  const errors = validationResult(req);
  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
    return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
  }
  // Proceed with signup
});
```

## 5. File Upload Security

**Issue**: The application allows arbitrary file uploads without proper content validation or scanning.

**Solution**: 
- Implement file type validation beyond just the extension
- Consider virus/malware scanning for uploaded files
- Set strict size limits per file type
```javascript
const upload = multer({
  storage: storage,
  limits: { fileSize: 25 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024 },
  fileFilter: (req, file, cb) => {
    // Check file type more thoroughly
    if (!allowedMimeTypes.includes(file.mimetype)) {
      return cb(new Error('Invalid file type'));
    }
    cb(null, true);
  }
});
```

## 6. Verbose Error Messages and Logging

**Issue**: Detailed error messages and logs could leak sensitive information.

**Solution**: Implement proper error handling with sanitized client-facing errors while maintaining detailed logs securely.
```javascript
// For client
res.status(500).json({ error: 'An error occurred' });

// For logs (with structured logging)
console.error('Upload processing error:', {
  error: error.message,
  stack: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? error.stack : undefined,
  user: req.username
});
```

## 7. Lack of Rate Limiting

**Issue**: No rate limiting for login attempts, uploads, or API requests.

**Solution**: Implement rate limiting for all endpoints, especially authentication.
```javascript
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');

const loginLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 5, // 5 attempts per IP
  message: { error: 'Too many login attempts, please try again later' }
});

app.post('/login', loginLimiter, (req, res) => {
  // Login logic
});
```

## 8. Weak Content Security Policy

**Issue**: The Content-Security-Policy header in nginx.conf allows 'unsafe-inline' and 'unsafe-eval'.

**Solution**: Strengthen the CSP by removing unsafe directives and using nonces or hashes for inline scripts when necessary.
```
add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self'; style-src 'self'; img-src 'self' data:;" always;
```

## 9. Missing Authentication for File Downloads

**Issue**: File downloads only check if the file exists and hasn't expired, without verifying the requester's identity.

**Solution**: Add authentication for file downloads or implement signed URLs with expiry for shared files.
```javascript
// For authenticated downloads
app.get('/download/:fileId', authenticateSession, handleDownload);

// For public shares, use signed URLs
const generateSignedUrl = (fileId) => {
  const expiry = Date.now() + (60 * 60 * 1000); // 1 hour
  const signature = crypto.createHmac('sha256', SECRET_KEY)
    .update(`${fileId}:${expiry}`)
    .digest('hex');
  return `/download/${fileId}?signature=${signature}&expiry=${expiry}`;
};
```

## 10. Insecure Data Storage

**Issue**: Sensitive data files (users.json, sessions.json) have no access controls beyond file system permissions.

**Solution**: Encrypt sensitive data at rest and implement proper access controls.
```javascript
const encryptData = (data, key) => {
  const iv = crypto.randomBytes(16);
  const cipher = crypto.createCipheriv('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);
  let encrypted = cipher.update(JSON.stringify(data), 'utf8', 'hex');
  encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
  const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
  return { encrypted, iv: iv.toString('hex'), authTag: authTag.toString('hex') };
};

// When saving data
const encryptedData = encryptData(Object.fromEntries(users), ENCRYPTION_KEY);
fs.writeFileSync('data/users.enc.json', JSON.stringify(encryptedData));
```

## 11. Lack of Security Headers

**Issue**: While some security headers are implemented in nginx, others are missing.

**Solution**: Add additional security headers like Permissions-Policy and improve existing ones.
```
add_header Permissions-Policy "geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()";
add_header X-Content-Type-Options "nosniff" always;
add_header Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy "same-origin" always;
add_header Cross-Origin-Embedder-Policy "require-corp" always;
```

## 12. No Secure Coding Practices Documentation

**Issue**: No clear documentation for developers on secure coding practices for this application.

**Solution**: Create a SECURITY.md file with guidelines for secure development and contribution.

## 13. Excessive Permissions in System Service

**Issue**: While the service file includes some security measures, it could be further restricted.

**Solution**: Add more restrictive systemd security options:
```
CapabilityBoundingSet=
RestrictAddressFamilies=AF_UNIX AF_INET AF_INET6
RestrictNamespaces=true
MemoryDenyWriteExecute=true
```

## 14. Missing Protection Against Common Web Vulnerabilities

**Issue**: No explicit protection against XSS, CSRF, and injection attacks in the application code.

**Solution**: 
- Implement CSRF tokens for all state-changing operations
- Use secure, HttpOnly, SameSite cookies
- Add a library like helmet.js for additional Express security
```javascript
const helmet = require('helmet');
app.use(helmet());

// For CSRF protection
const csrf = require('csurf');
const csrfProtection = csrf({ cookie: { 
  httpOnly: true, 
  secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
  sameSite: 'strict'
}});
app.use(csrfProtection);
```

## 15. Exposed User Data

**Issue**: User existence can be determined through the signup process.

**Solution**: Implement constant-time responses for user-related operations to prevent enumeration attacks.
```javascript
// Instead of:
if (users.has(username)) {
  return res.json({ success: false, error: 'Username already exists' });
}

// Use:
const result = await bcrypt.hash(password, saltRounds);
if (users.has(username)) {
  return res.json({ success: false, error: 'Registration failed' });
}
// Continue with registration
```

By addressing these security vulnerabilities, you'll significantly improve the security posture of your file sharing application. I recommend prioritizing the password storage, session management, and file upload security issues as they present the most immediate risks.

Jack

# Database implementation

### Sendi.fi “Scenario B” - one lean droplet + DigitalOcean Spaces

```
Browser / App
      │ 1  (POST /api/upload)
      ▼
┌────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Droplet  (2 vCPU · 4 GB · Ubuntu 22) │  $12/mo
│  • NGINX  ── TLS ▸ certbot            │
│  • Sendi.fi API  (Node / Go / …)      │
│  • SQLite (tiny metadata)             │
└────────┬──────────────────────────────┘
         │2. presigned URL JSON
         ▼
┌────────────────────────────────────────┐
│    Client uploads file **directly**    │
│   PUT /files-prod/…?X-Amz-Signature    │
└────────┬──────────────────────────────┘
         │3. GET for download (expiry ≤15 min)
         ▼
┌────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  DigitalOcean **Spaces** bucket        │  $5/mo
│  • Private ACL, AES-256 at rest        │
│  • Lifecycle rule: delete >24 h        │
└────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

## 1.  Provision cloud resources   (10 min)

| Step | Console action                                                                                             |
| ---- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| 1    | **Create → Droplet** → Basic • *2 vCPU / 4 GB / 80 GB* • Ubuntu 22 • enable monitoring & IPv6.             |
| 2    | **Create → Spaces** → Region ≠ same as droplet (latency) • name `files-prod` • *Restrict File Listing* ON. |
| 3    | **Generate Spaces key** (Settings → API) → note `SPACES_KEY` / `SPACES_SECRET`.                            |
| 4    | **Lifecycle rule**: *Add rule → Delete objects older than 1 day* → Save.                                   |
| 5    | Add **A-record** `files.yourdomain.com` → droplet IP.                                                      |

---

## 2.  Prepare the droplet   (20 min)

```bash
ssh root@YOUR_IP
apt update && apt -y install nginx certbot python3-certbot-nginx \
  unzip ufw fail2ban
ufw allow "OpenSSH"
ufw allow "Nginx Full"
ufw enable
adduser sendi && usermod -aG sudo sendi
```

### TLS & basic hardening

```bash
certbot --nginx -d files.yourdomain.com --email you@domain --agree-tos --non-interactive
sed -i 's/PasswordAuthentication yes/PasswordAuthentication no/' /etc/ssh/sshd_config
systemctl restart sshd
```

---

## 3.  Deploy the application   (15 min)

1. **Copy env vars** *(as root → `/etc/sendifi/.env` mode 600)*

   ```
   SPACES_ENDPOINT=https://nyc3.digitaloceanspaces.com
   SPACES_BUCKET=files-prod
   SPACES_KEY=xxxxxxxx
   SPACES_SECRET=yyyyyyyy
   BASE_URL=https://files.yourdomain.com
   ```

2. **Service unit** `/etc/systemd/system/sendifi.service`

   ```ini
   [Unit]  Description=Sendi.fi API
   [Service]
   User=sendi
   EnvironmentFile=/etc/sendifi/.env
   ExecStart=/usr/local/bin/sendifi
   Restart=on-failure
   [Install] WantedBy=multi-user.target
   ```

3. `systemctl daemon-reload && systemctl enable --now sendifi`

4. **Nginx site** `/etc/nginx/sites-available/sendifi`

   ```nginx
   server {
     listen 443 ssl;
     server_name files.yourdomain.com;
     ssl_certificate     /etc/letsencrypt/live/files.yourdomain.com/fullchain.pem;
     ssl_certificate_key /etc/letsencrypt/live/files.yourdomain.com/privkey.pem;

     location /api/ {
       proxy_pass http://127.0.0.1:3000/;
       proxy_set_header Host $host;
       proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
     }
   }
   ```

   Enable: `ln -s /etc/nginx/sites-available/sendifi /etc/nginx/sites-enabled && nginx -t && systemctl reload nginx`

---

## 4.  App-side S3 code snippet   (typescript)

```ts
import { S3Client, CreatePresignedPostCommand } from "@aws-sdk/client-s3";
import { createPresignedPost } from "@aws-sdk/s3-presigned-post";

const s3 = new S3Client({
  credentials: { accessKeyId: P.SPACES_KEY, secretAccessKey: P.SPACES_SECRET },
  endpoint: P.SPACES_ENDPOINT,
  region: "us-east-1", // fixed for Spaces
});

export async function createUpload(userId: string, mime: string, bytes: number) {
  const key = `u/${userId}/${crypto.randomUUID()}`;
  const presign = await createPresignedPost(s3, {
    Bucket: P.SPACES_BUCKET,
    Key: key,
    Conditions: [["content-length-range", 0, 104857600]], // 100 MB max
    Expires: 900, // 15 min
  });
  await db("files").insert({ key, user_id: userId, mime, bytes, expires: now + 86400 });
  return presign;       // JSON back to client
}
```

---

## 5.  House-keeping cron   (2 min)

```bash
echo "0 * * * * sendi sqlite3 /home/sendi/metadata.db \
  'DELETE FROM files WHERE expires < strftime(\"%s\",\"now\");'" \
  | sudo tee /etc/cron.d/sendifi-expire
```

Spaces auto-deletes blobs; cron just prunes the tiny SQLite rows.

---

## 6.  Monitoring & alerts   (5 min)

* **DigitalOcean Monitoring**:
  *Droplet* → *Create alert*: CPU > 70 % (10 min), Disk > 80 %.
* **fail2ban** already blocks brute-force SSH.
* Enable **Spaces usage logs** if you need audit: *Spaces → Settings → Usage Logging → target bucket*.

---

## 7.  Cost recap

| Item                          | Monthly  |
| ----------------------------- | -------- |
| Droplet 2 vCPU / 4 GB         | \$12     |
| DigitalOcean Spaces (≤250 GB) | \$5      |
| **Total**                     | **\$17** |

---

### Timeline checklist

| Day         | Goal                                                                                       |
| ----------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| **0**       | Provision droplet & Spaces; run boiler-plate above → service live.                         |
| **+1**      | Smoke-test uploads/downloads; verify 24 h auto-delete.                                     |
| **+7**      | Turn on firewall logs & review certbot auto-renew.                                         |
| **Monthly** | `doctl compute droplet-action snapshot` + download or replicate Space if you need backups. |

That’s the entire implementation. Add managed PostgreSQL or Redis later with the same presigned-URL flow if you need richer features, but you can serve 500 users securely today with just these two DigitalOcean services.

# PRD

1. Overview
1.1 Purpose
You have a dataset of ~2000 nonprofit organizations in an Excel (XLSX) file. The goal is to automate finding each nonprofit’s website and insert that information into a new column. If no website can be found, those entries will be left blank or skipped.

1.2 Objectives
Automate Data Enrichment: Eliminate manual searching and data entry.
Maintain Data Accuracy: Only insert valid URLs.
Save Time & Resources: Ensure efficient and fast processing of 2000+ nonprofits.
2. Scope
2.1 In-Scope
File Ingestion: Reading a local XLSX file containing nonprofits’ identifying information (e.g., name, location).
Website Discovery: Use programmatic methods (e.g., a search engine API or a third-party database/API) to find each nonprofit’s official website.
Data Output: Write the discovered URLs to a new column in the original XLSX file (or a new file).
Error Handling: If a website is not found or no valid link is available, skip or leave blank.
2.2 Out-of-Scope
Advanced Validation: Deep verification of site correctness beyond standard checks (e.g., verifying page content).
Data Cleansing: The script will not perform extensive data cleaning on nonprofits’ names or addresses (beyond simple trimming/casing).
User Interface: This will be a script/CLI tool with no dedicated GUI.
3. Functional Requirements
Read Input File

Input: An XLSX file with at least the following columns:
Nonprofit Name
(Optional) City, State, or other location details
Process: Script should parse rows in the designated sheet.
Generate Search Terms

For each row, the script will use the nonprofit name (and potentially location) to form a search query.
Search/Lookup Website

Approach A: Use a search engine API (e.g., Google Custom Search, Bing Search API) to retrieve the official homepage.
Approach B: Use a third-party nonprofit directory API if available.
Validation:
Make sure the URL format is valid (e.g., starts with http/https).
Optional check: Compare domain to nonprofit name for basic validation.
Write to Output

New Column: Add or update the XLSX with a new column, e.g., “Website.”
If no website is found, leave the cell blank or skip.
Logging & Error Handling

Logging: Keep a simple log file or console output to track:
Number of nonprofits processed
Successful URLs found
Nonprofits with no website found
Error Handling:
Handle API connection failures with retries or skip gracefully.
If a row is missing key data, skip or log an error.
4. Non-Functional Requirements
Performance

Must handle ~2000 rows in a single run without timing out or crashing.
Use lightweight libraries or asynchronous requests to speed up API calls (if required).
Scalability

The script should be easy to modify for additional columns (e.g., contact info, social media links) in the future.
Security

API keys and credentials must be secured in environment variables or a secure configuration file, not hard-coded.
The script should not expose sensitive information in logs.
Maintainability

Code should be well-documented and modular (e.g., separate functions for file handling, search, data processing, etc.).
Use commonly supported and updated libraries for XLSX parsing (e.g., openpyxl in Python, or a similar library in Node.js).
5. Technical Approach & Dependencies
Language/Platform

Python (commonly used for data tasks, strong library support) or Node.js (equally feasible).
Alternatively, any language that supports RESTful calls and XLSX handling.
Libraries & Tools

Python:
openpyxl or pandas for XLSX reading/writing
requests or httpx for handling API calls
Node.js:
xlsx (SheetJS) for file handling
axios or node-fetch for API calls
Search API

Google Custom Search, Bing Search, or similar.
Must handle API key usage and possible usage limits.
Infrastructure

Script can run locally or on a cloud environment (e.g., AWS Lambda, Azure Functions, Docker container).
6. Milestones & Deliverables
MVP
Script can read XLSX, find websites via a single approach (search engine or known directory), and write output.
Enhanced
Implement error handling, logging, and optional domain validation.
Deployment
Document instructions for running the script in a production or local environment.
7. Acceptance Criteria
Correctness
For at least 80% of nonprofits with known websites, the script finds valid URLs.
Completeness
All ~2000 rows are processed without unrecoverable errors.
Output Validity
Final XLSX file includes a “Website” column with the correct URL or empty cells if not found.
Performance
Script finishes within a reasonable time (e.g., under 30 minutes for 2000 records with a typical API rate limit).
8. Risks & Mitigations
API Rate Limits

Risk: Hitting search engine API limits with 2000 queries.
Mitigation: Use caching or batch queries. Investigate higher-tier subscription if needed.
Incomplete Data

Risk: Missing or incorrect nonprofit names hamper search accuracy.
Mitigation: Implement minimal data cleaning and allow partial matches, or skip on repeated failures.
Maintenance Overhead

Risk: Changing APIs or XLSX formats might break the script.
Mitigation: Keep code modular, track dependencies, and update when new versions are released.

# PRD

🛠 Product Requirements Document: Open Source Mail Merge (OSMM)
📌 Product Name (Working Title): MailMerge+
1. Overview
MailMerge+ is an open-source Google Workspace add-on that allows users to send personalized email campaigns directly from Gmail using data from Google Sheets. It offers a privacy-first, cost-free alternative to commercial mail merge solutions like YAMM, focused on transparency, extensibility, and community contribution.

2. Goals
Allow non-technical users to send personalized emails from Gmail using a Google Sheet.

Enable open collaboration and contribution from developers.

Avoid daily email limits where possible by batching or queuing intelligently.

Respect privacy: No third-party tracking or data sharing.

Provide extensibility for developers to add custom logic or integrations (e.g., via Apps Script triggers or GitHub Actions).

3. Key Features
✅ MVP Features
Feature	Description
Google Sheets Add-on	UI button to trigger mail merge (custom sidebar or menu).
Gmail Draft as Template	Pick a draft from user’s Gmail as the email template.
Placeholder Replacement	Replace {{column_name}} tags with values from each row.
Status Column	Track "SENT", "ERROR", or "QUEUED" per recipient in the sheet.
Attachments	Optional: add PDF attachments via Drive links.
Throttling Support	Enforce Gmail limits (e.g., 100–150/day for free users, 1500+ for Workspace).
Logs	Add basic logging in a dedicated Google Sheet tab.
Permissions	Use only minimal permissions (email, sheets, compose).
🚀 Stretch Features
Feature	Description
Scheduled Send	Schedule campaigns using Sheets + Apps Script triggers.
Open Tracking (Optional)	Add a lightweight pixel tracker (self-hosted only).
Google Form Integration	Auto-send emails when a Form is submitted.
Email Preview	Show merged email preview before sending.
CSV Export	Export campaign results: emails, statuses, errors.
Gmail Labeling	Automatically apply a label to sent emails for tracking.
Custom Add-on Branding	Option for organizations to white-label the add-on.
4. Target Users
Educators: Teachers sending emails to students or parents.

Small Businesses / Nonprofits: Running donation or customer campaigns.

Event Organizers: Managing RSVPs and reminders.

Open Source Enthusiasts: Looking for a privacy-focused alternative.

5. Tech Stack
Component	Tech
Frontend UI	Google Sheets Add-on UI (Google Apps Script HTMLService)
Backend Logic	Google Apps Script
Email Engine	Gmail API via Apps Script
Storage	Google Sheets
Auth	Google OAuth Scopes (minimal: email, compose, read-only drive access)
Optional Hosting	GitHub Pages for documentation; Firebase or Supabase for enhancements
6. Permissions Required
https://www.googleapis.com/auth/script.container.ui – UI integration

https://www.googleapis.com/auth/spreadsheets – Read/write data

https://www.googleapis.com/auth/gmail.compose – Send emails

https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.readonly – (Optional) Attachment support
