# Reference analytics 

// LSATAnalyticsDashboard.tsx

import React, { useState, useMemo, useEffect } from 'react';
import { LineChart, Line, BarChart, Bar, XAxis, YAxis, CartesianGrid, Tooltip, Legend, ResponsiveContainer, PieChart, Pie, Cell } from 'recharts';
import { Tab, Tabs, TabList, TabPanel } from 'react-tabs';
import 'react-tabs/style/react-tabs.css'; // Basic styling for tabs

// Helper to generate a unique ID (in a real app, use a library like uuid)
let idCounter = 0;
const uniqueId = () => `id_${idCounter++}`;

//region 1. Type Definitions (types.ts)
//=============================================================================
interface QuestionAttempt {
  id: string;
  timestamp: string; // ISO date string
  section: 'LR' | 'RC'; // Simplified to LR & RC as per primary focus
  questionType: string;
  isCorrect: boolean;
  timeSpentSeconds: number;
  difficulty: 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5;
  logicType?: 'comparative' | 'conditional' | 'causal' | 'other'; // For LR questions
}

interface QuestionTypeFrequency {
  [questionType: string]: number; // e.g., "Assumption": 0.15 (15% of LR questions in general)
}

interface Drill {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  targetsLogicType?: 'comparative' | 'conditional' | 'causal';
  targetsQuestionType?: string;
  link: string; // Link to the drill
}

type TimeFilterOption = 'all' | 'month' | 'week' | 'day';

//endregion

//region 2. Mock Data (mockData.ts)
//=============================================================================
const MOCK_QUESTION_TYPES_LR = ["Assumption", "Strengthen", "Weaken", "Inference", "Flaw", "Main Point", "Principle", "Paradox"];
const MOCK_QUESTION_TYPES_RC = ["Main Idea", "Detail", "Inference RC", "Structure", "Author's Tone"];

const MOCK_QUESTION_TYPE_FREQUENCIES: QuestionTypeFrequency = {
  "Assumption": 0.18, "Strengthen": 0.15, "Weaken": 0.15, "Inference": 0.12, "Flaw": 0.10,
  "Main Point": 0.08, "Principle": 0.07, "Paradox": 0.05, "Must Be True": 0.10,
  // RC Frequencies (less standardized, example)
  "Main Idea": 0.25, "Detail": 0.30, "Inference RC": 0.20, "Structure": 0.15, "Author's Tone": 0.10,
};

const MOCK_DRILLS: Drill[] = [
  { id: 'd1', title: 'Conditional Logic Mastery', description: 'Practice identifying and diagramming conditional statements.', targetsLogicType: 'conditional', link: '#drill-conditional' },
  { id: 'd2', title: 'Causal Flaw Spotting', description: 'Learn to spot common causal reasoning errors.', targetsLogicType: 'causal', link: '#drill-causal' },
  { id: 'd3', title: 'Comparative Analysis Workout', description: 'Exercises for distinguishing and evaluating comparative claims.', targetsLogicType: 'comparative', link: '#drill-comparative' },
  { id: 'd4', title: 'Assumption Question Deep Dive', description: 'Focused practice on Assumption questions.', targetsQuestionType: 'Assumption', link: '#drill-assumption' },
  { id: 'd5', title: 'Strengthen/Weaken Core Skills', description: 'Build your ability to identify arguments that strengthen or weaken conclusions.', targetsQuestionType: 'Strengthen', link: '#drill-strengthen-weaken' }
];

const generateMockAttempts = (numAttempts: number): QuestionAttempt[] => {
  const attempts: QuestionAttempt[] = [];
  const startDate = new Date();
  startDate.setFullYear(startDate.getFullYear() - 1); // Up to 1 year ago

  for (let i = 0; i < numAttempts; i++) {
    const section = Math.random() < 0.7 ? 'LR' : 'RC'; // More LR than RC
    const questionTypes = section === 'LR' ? MOCK_QUESTION_TYPES_LR : MOCK_QUESTION_TYPES_RC;
    const questionType = questionTypes[Math.floor(Math.random() * questionTypes.length)];
    const logicTypes: QuestionAttempt['logicType'][] = ['comparative', 'conditional', 'causal', 'other'];

    attempts.push({
      id: uniqueId(),
      timestamp: new Date(startDate.getTime() + Math.random() * (Date.now() - startDate.getTime())).toISOString(),
      section: section,
      questionType: questionType,
      isCorrect: Math.random() < (0.4 + i / (numAttempts * 2)), // Slightly improving over time
      timeSpentSeconds: Math.floor(Math.random() * 120) + 30, // 30s to 150s
      difficulty: (Math.floor(Math.random() * 5) + 1) as QuestionAttempt['difficulty'],
      logicType: section === 'LR' ? logicTypes[Math.floor(Math.random() * logicTypes.length)] : undefined,
    });
  }
  return attempts.sort((a, b) => new Date(a.timestamp).getTime() - new Date(b.timestamp).getTime());
};

const ALL_MOCK_ATTEMPTS: QuestionAttempt[] = generateMockAttempts(500); // Generate 500 mock attempts

//endregion

//region 3. Utility Functions (utils.ts)
//=============================================================================
const filterAttemptsByTime = (attempts: QuestionAttempt[], filter: TimeFilterOption): QuestionAttempt[] => {
  const now = new Date();
  let cutoffDate = new Date(0); // Start of epoch for 'all'

  if (filter === 'month') {
    cutoffDate = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth() - 1, now.getDate());
  } else if (filter === 'week') {
    cutoffDate = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), now.getDate() - 7);
  } else if (filter === 'day') {
    cutoffDate = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), now.getDate() - 1);
  }

  return attempts.filter(attempt => new Date(attempt.timestamp) >= cutoffDate);
};

const calculateAccuracy = (attempts: QuestionAttempt[]): number => {
  if (attempts.length === 0) return 0;
  const correctCount = attempts.filter(a => a.isCorrect).length;
  return (correctCount / attempts.length) * 100;
};

const groupAttemptsBy = <K extends keyof any>(attempts: QuestionAttempt[], keySelector: (attempt: QuestionAttempt) => K) => {
  return attempts.reduce((acc, attempt) => {
    const key = keySelector(attempt);
    if (!acc[key]) {
      acc[key] = [];
    }
    acc[key].push(attempt);
    return acc;
  }, {} as Record<K, QuestionAttempt[]>);
};

const getMotivationalMessage = (accuracy?: number): string => {
  if (accuracy === undefined) return "Keep practicing! Every question is a learning opportunity.";
  if (accuracy >= 80) return "Outstanding work! Your dedication is paying off. Keep pushing!";
  if (accuracy >= 60) return "Great progress! You're building a strong foundation. Stay consistent!";
  if (accuracy >= 40) return "You're on the right track! Identify those tricky areas and focus on them. You can do it!";
  return "The LSAT is challenging, but you're tougher. Review your mistakes, learn from them, and remember how far you've come!";
};

//endregion

//region 4. UI Components (components/*)
//=============================================================================

//region Shared Components
//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
interface TimeFilterProps {
  selectedFilter: TimeFilterOption;
  onFilterChange: (filter: TimeFilterOption) => void;
}

const TimeFilter: React.FC<TimeFilterProps> = ({ selectedFilter, onFilterChange }) => {
  const filters: { label: string; value: TimeFilterOption }[] = [
    { label: 'All Time', value: 'all' },
    { label: 'Last Month', value: 'month' },
    { label: 'Last Week', value: 'week' },
    { label: 'Last 24 Hours', value: 'day' },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="time-filter-controls mb-6 flex justify-center space-x-2">
      {filters.map(f => (
        <button
          key={f.value}
          onClick={() => onFilterChange(f.value)}
          className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors
            ${selectedFilter === f.value ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-300 text-gray-700'}`}
        >
          {f.label}
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};

const Card: React.FC<{ title: string; children: React.ReactNode; className?: string }> = ({ title, children, className }) => (
  <div className={`bg-white shadow-lg rounded-xl p-6 ${className || ''}`}>
    <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-700 mb-4">{title}</h3>
    {children}
  </div>
);

const ChartContainer: React.FC<{ title: string; children: React.ReactNode; height?: number | string }> = ({ title, children, height = 300 }) => (
  <Card title={title}>
    <div style={{ width: '100%', height }}>
      {children}
    </div>
  </Card>
);

const MotivationalMessageDisplay: React.FC<{ message?: string; accuracy?: number }> = ({ message, accuracy }) => {
  const displayedMessage = message || getMotivationalMessage(accuracy);
  return (
    <div className="my-6 p-4 bg-blue-100 border-l-4 border-blue-500 text-blue-700 rounded-md">
      <p className="font-medium">A quick thought:</p>
      <p>{displayedMessage}</p>
    </div>
  );
};
//endregion Shared Components

//region OverallPerformanceTab
//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
interface OverallPerformanceTabProps {
  attempts: QuestionAttempt[];
}

const OverallPerformanceTab: React.FC<OverallPerformanceTabProps> = ({ attempts }) => {
  const lrAttempts = useMemo(() => attempts.filter(a => a.section === 'LR'), [attempts]);
  const rcAttempts = useMemo(() => attempts.filter(a => a.section === 'RC'), [attempts]);

  const overallLRAccuracy = useMemo(() => calculateAccuracy(lrAttempts), [lrAttempts]);
  const overallRCAccuracy = useMemo(() => calculateAccuracy(rcAttempts), [rcAttempts]);

  const trendData = useMemo(() => {
    if (attempts.length === 0) return [];
    // Simple trend: divide time period into 5-10 points
    const sortedAttempts = [...attempts].sort((a,b) => new Date(a.timestamp).getTime() - new Date(b.timestamp).getTime());
    const numPoints = Math.min(10, Math.floor(sortedAttempts.length / 5)); // Max 10 points, min 1 point per 5 attempts
    if (numPoints < 2) { // Need at least 2 points for a line
        if(sortedAttempts.length > 0) {
            const midDate = new Date(sortedAttempts[0].timestamp);
            return [{
                name: midDate.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' }),
                LR: calculateAccuracy(sortedAttempts.filter(a => a.section === 'LR')),
                RC: calculateAccuracy(sortedAttempts.filter(a => a.section === 'RC')),
            }];
        }
        return [];
    }

    const points = [];
    const totalDuration = new Date(sortedAttempts[sortedAttempts.length - 1].timestamp).getTime() - new Date(sortedAttempts[0].timestamp).getTime();
    const interval = totalDuration / (numPoints -1);
    
    let currentIntervalStart = new Date(sortedAttempts[0].timestamp).getTime();

    for (let i = 0; i < numPoints; i++) {
        const intervalEnd = currentIntervalStart + interval;
        const attemptsInInterval = sortedAttempts.filter(a => {
            const t = new Date(a.timestamp).getTime();
            return t >= currentIntervalStart && (i === numPoints - 1 ? t <= intervalEnd : t < intervalEnd); // include end for last point
        });
        
        const lrInInterval = attemptsInInterval.filter(a => a.section === 'LR');
        const rcInInterval = attemptsInInterval.filter(a => a.section === 'RC');

        const dateForLabel = new Date(currentIntervalStart + interval / 2);

        points.push({
            name: dateForLabel.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' }),
            LR: lrInInterval.length > 0 ? calculateAccuracy(lrInInterval) : null, // Use null for recharts to break line if no data
            RC: rcInInterval.length > 0 ? calculateAccuracy(rcInInterval) : null,
        });
        currentIntervalStart = intervalEnd;
    }
    return points.filter(p => p.LR !== null || p.RC !== null); // Filter out points with no data at all
  }, [attempts]);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <MotivationalMessageDisplay accuracy={(overallLRAccuracy + overallRCAccuracy) / 2} />
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
        <Card title="Logical Reasoning (LR) Overall">
          <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-blue-600">{overallLRAccuracy.toFixed(1)}%</p>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">{lrAttempts.length} questions attempted</p>
        </Card>
        <Card title="Reading Comprehension (RC) Overall">
          <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-green-600">{overallRCAccuracy.toFixed(1)}%</p>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">{rcAttempts.length} questions attempted</p>
        </Card>
      </div>

      <ChartContainer title="Accuracy Trends Over Time">
        <ResponsiveContainer>
          <LineChart data={trendData} margin={{ top: 5, right: 20, left: -20, bottom: 5 }}>
            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" />
            <XAxis dataKey="name" />
            <YAxis domain={[0, 100]} unit="%" />
            <Tooltip />
            <Legend />
            <Line type="monotone" dataKey="LR" stroke="#3B82F6" strokeWidth={2} connectNulls={true} name="LR Accuracy" />
            <Line type="monotone" dataKey="RC" stroke="#10B981" strokeWidth={2} connectNulls={true} name="RC Accuracy" />
          </LineChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer>
      </ChartContainer>

      <RecentActivityFeed attempts={attempts.slice(-10).reverse()} />
    </div>
  );
};
//endregion OverallPerformanceTab

//region QuestionTypeTab
//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
interface QuestionTypeTabProps {
  attempts: QuestionAttempt[];
  frequencies: QuestionTypeFrequency;
}

const QuestionTypeTab: React.FC<QuestionTypeTabProps> = ({ attempts, frequencies }) => {
  const performanceByQuestionType = useMemo(() => {
    const grouped = groupAttemptsBy(attempts, a => `${a.section}-${a.questionType}`);
    return Object.entries(grouped).map(([key, typeAttempts]) => {
      const [section, questionType] = key.split('-');
      const total = typeAttempts.length;
      const correct = typeAttempts.filter(a => a.isCorrect).length;
      const incorrect = total - correct;
      const accuracy = total > 0 ? (correct / total) * 100 : 0;
      const percentIncorrect = total > 0 ? (incorrect / total) : 0; // Use as decimal for formula
      
      // Frequency might be section-specific in a more complex model
      // For now, use general frequency, or filter if section is LR
      const frequencyOnExam = frequencies[questionType] || 0.01; // Default low frequency if not found

      const priorityScore = frequencyOnExam * percentIncorrect * 100; // Multiply by 100 for better scale

      return {
        section,
        questionType,
        total,
        correct,
        accuracy,
        priorityScore: parseFloat(priorityScore.toFixed(2)) // Keep it neat
      };
    }).sort((a,b) => b.priorityScore - a.priorityScore); // Sort by priority score descending
  }, [attempts, frequencies]);

  const lrQuestionTypes = performanceByQuestionType.filter(item => item.section === 'LR');
  const rcQuestionTypes = performanceByQuestionType.filter(item => item.section === 'RC');

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <MotivationalMessageDisplay message="Understanding your strengths and weaknesses by question type is key to smart studying. Focus on high-priority areas first!" />
      
      <Card title="Question Type Priority (LR)">
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-2">
          Prioritized by: (Frequency on Exam × % Incorrect). Higher score means higher priority.
        </p>
        {lrQuestionTypes.length > 0 ? (
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Type</th>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Accuracy</th>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Attempted</th>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Priority Score</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {lrQuestionTypes.map(item => (
                  <tr key={`lr-${item.questionType}`}>
                    <td className="px-4 py-2 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{item.questionType}</td>
                    <td className={`px-4 py-2 whitespace-nowrap text-sm ${item.accuracy >= 70 ? 'text-green-600' : item.accuracy >= 50 ? 'text-yellow-600' : 'text-red-600'}`}>{item.accuracy.toFixed(1)}%</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-2 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-500">{item.total}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-2 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-semibold text-blue-600">{item.priorityScore.toFixed(2)}</td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        ) : <p className="text-gray-500">Not enough LR data for this period.</p>}
      </Card>

      <ChartContainer title="LR Question Type Performance">
        <ResponsiveContainer>
          <BarChart data={lrQuestionTypes.slice(0,10)} layout="vertical" margin={{ top: 5, right: 30, left: 50, bottom: 5 }}>
            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" />
            <XAxis type="number" domain={[0, 100]} unit="%" />
            <YAxis dataKey="questionType" type="category" width={100} interval={0} />
            <Tooltip formatter={(value: number) => `${value.toFixed(1)}%`} />
            <Legend />
            <Bar dataKey="accuracy" name="Accuracy" fill="#3B82F6" />
          </BarChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer>
      </ChartContainer>

       <Card title="Question Type Performance (RC)">
        {rcQuestionTypes.length > 0 ? (
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
               <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Type</th>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Accuracy</th>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Attempted</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {rcQuestionTypes.sort((a,b)=> b.accuracy - a.accuracy).map(item => ( // Sort by accuracy here
                  <tr key={`rc-${item.questionType}`}>
                    <td className="px-4 py-2 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{item.questionType}</td>
                    <td className={`px-4 py-2 whitespace-nowrap text-sm ${item.accuracy >= 70 ? 'text-green-600' : item.accuracy >= 50 ? 'text-yellow-600' : 'text-red-600'}`}>{item.accuracy.toFixed(1)}%</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-2 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-500">{item.total}</td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        ) : <p className="text-gray-500">Not enough RC data for this period.</p>}
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
};
//endregion QuestionTypeTab

//region DifficultyLogicTab
//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
interface DifficultyLogicTabProps {
  attempts: QuestionAttempt[];
  drills: Drill[];
}

const DifficultyLogicTab: React.FC<DifficultyLogicTabProps> = ({ attempts, drills }) => {
  const performanceByDifficulty = useMemo(() => {
    const grouped = groupAttemptsBy(attempts, a => a.difficulty);
    return Object.entries(grouped).map(([difficulty, diffAttempts]) => ({
      difficulty: `Level ${difficulty}`,
      accuracy: calculateAccuracy(diffAttempts),
      total: diffAttempts.length,
      avgTime: diffAttempts.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.timeSpentSeconds, 0) / diffAttempts.length || 0
    })).sort((a,b) => parseInt(a.difficulty.split(' ')[1]) - parseInt(b.difficulty.split(' ')[1]));
  }, [attempts]);

  const lrAttempts = useMemo(() => attempts.filter(a => a.section === 'LR' && a.logicType), [attempts]);
  const logicTypePerformance = useMemo(() => {
    const groupedByLogic = groupAttemptsBy(lrAttempts.filter(a => a.logicType && a.logicType !== 'other'), a => a.logicType!);
    return (['conditional', 'causal', 'comparative'] as const).map(logicType => {
        const typeAttempts = groupedByLogic[logicType] || [];
        const total = typeAttempts.length;
        const incorrect = typeAttempts.filter(a => !a.isCorrect).length;
        return {
            name: logicType.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + logicType.slice(1),
            total,
            incorrect,
            percentIncorrect: total > 0 ? (incorrect / total) * 100 : 0
        };
    }).filter(lt => lt.total > 0).sort((a,b) => b.percentIncorrect - a.percentIncorrect); // Highest % incorrect first
  }, [lrAttempts]);

  const recommendedDrills = useMemo(() => {
    const recommendations: Drill[] = [];
    const addedDrillIds = new Set<string>();

    // Recommend based on logic type errors
    logicTypePerformance.slice(0, 2).forEach(lt => { // Top 2 problematic logic types
      if (lt.percentIncorrect > 30) { // Only if significant error rate
        const drill = drills.find(d => d.targetsLogicType === lt.name.toLowerCase());
        if (drill && !addedDrillIds.has(drill.id)) {
          recommendations.push(drill);
          addedDrillIds.add(drill.id);
        }
      }
    });
    // Could add more logic for question type specific drills if needed
    if (recommendations.length < 2 && drills.length > 0) { // Fill with general drills if not enough specific
        drills.forEach(d => {
            if(recommendations.length < 2 && !addedDrillIds.has(d.id)){
                recommendations.push(d);
                addedDrillIds.add(d.id);
            }
        })
    }
    return recommendations.slice(0,3); // Max 3 drills
  }, [logicTypePerformance, drills]);

  const COLORS_DIFFICULTY = ['#0088FE', '#00C49F', '#FFBB28', '#FF8042', '#FF4F5E'];

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <MotivationalMessageDisplay message="Challenge is part of the growth. Notice how your performance changes with difficulty and where your reasoning patterns lie." />
      
      <ChartContainer title="Performance by Question Difficulty">
        <ResponsiveContainer>
          <BarChart data={performanceByDifficulty}>
            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" />
            <XAxis dataKey="difficulty" />
            <YAxis yAxisId="left" orientation="left" stroke="#8884d8" domain={[0,100]} unit="%" />
            <YAxis yAxisId="right" orientation="right" stroke="#82ca9d" unit="s" />
            <Tooltip />
            <Legend />
            <Bar yAxisId="left" dataKey="accuracy" name="Accuracy" fill="#8884d8">
                {performanceByDifficulty.map((entry, index) => (
                    <Cell key={`cell-${index}`} fill={COLORS_DIFFICULTY[index % COLORS_DIFFICULTY.length]} />
                ))}
            </Bar>
            <Bar yAxisId="right" dataKey="avgTime" name="Avg. Time (s)" fill="#82ca9d" />
          </BarChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer>
      </ChartContainer>

      <Card title="LR Logic Type Hotspots (% Incorrect)">
        {logicTypePerformance.length > 0 ? (
            <div className="space-y-3">
                {logicTypePerformance.map(lt => (
                    <div key={lt.name} className="p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-md">
                        <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                            <span className="font-medium text-gray-700">{lt.name} Logic</span>
                            <span className={`font-semibold ${lt.percentIncorrect > 50 ? 'text-red-500' : 'text-yellow-600'}`}>
                                {lt.percentIncorrect.toFixed(1)}% incorrect
                            </span>
                        </div>
                        <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2.5 mt-1">
                            <div className="bg-red-500 h-2.5 rounded-full" style={{ width: `${lt.percentIncorrect}%` }}></div>
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">{lt.incorrect} incorrect out of {lt.total} questions.</p>
                    </div>
                ))}
            </div>
        ) : <p className="text-gray-500">Not enough LR data with logic types for this period.</p>}
      </Card>

      {recommendedDrills.length > 0 && (
        <Card title="Recommended Drills">
          <ul className="space-y-3">
            {recommendedDrills.map(drill => (
              <li key={drill.id} className="p-3 border border-gray-200 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors">
                <h4 className="font-semibold text-blue-600">{drill.title}</h4>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-1">{drill.description}</p>
                <a href={drill.link} className="text-sm text-blue-500 hover:underline">Start Drill →</a>
              </li>
            ))}
          </ul>
        </Card>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};
//endregion DifficultyLogicTab

//region TimingAnalysisTab
//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
interface TimingAnalysisTabProps {
  attempts: QuestionAttempt[];
}
const TimingAnalysisTab: React.FC<TimingAnalysisTabProps> = ({ attempts }) => {
  const timingData = useMemo(() => {
    const lrAttempts = attempts.filter(a => a.section === 'LR');
    const rcAttempts = attempts.filter(a => a.section === 'RC');

    const avgTimeLR = lrAttempts.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.timeSpentSeconds, 0) / (lrAttempts.length || 1);
    const avgTimeRC = rcAttempts.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.timeSpentSeconds, 0) / (rcAttempts.length || 1);

    const avgTimeCorrectLR = lrAttempts.filter(a=>a.isCorrect).reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.timeSpentSeconds, 0) / (lrAttempts.filter(a=>a.isCorrect).length || 1);
    const avgTimeIncorrectLR = lrAttempts.filter(a=>!a.isCorrect).reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.timeSpentSeconds, 0) / (lrAttempts.filter(a=>!a.isCorrect).length || 1);
    
    const avgTimeCorrectRC = rcAttempts.filter(a=>a.isCorrect).reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.timeSpentSeconds, 0) / (rcAttempts.filter(a=>a.isCorrect).length || 1);
    const avgTimeIncorrectRC = rcAttempts.filter(a=>!a.isCorrect).reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.timeSpentSeconds, 0) / (rcAttempts.filter(a=>!a.isCorrect).length || 1);

    const byQuestionType = Object.entries(groupAttemptsBy(attempts, a => a.questionType))
      .map(([questionType, qtAttempts]) => {
        const avgTime = qtAttempts.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.timeSpentSeconds, 0) / (qtAttempts.length || 1);
        const avgTimeCorrect = qtAttempts.filter(a=>a.isCorrect).reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.timeSpentSeconds, 0) / (qtAttempts.filter(a=>a.isCorrect).length || 1);
        const avgTimeIncorrect = qtAttempts.filter(a=>!a.isCorrect).reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.timeSpentSeconds, 0) / (qtAttempts.filter(a=>!a.isCorrect).length || 1);
        return {
          questionType,
          avgTime: parseFloat(avgTime.toFixed(1)),
          avgTimeCorrect: parseFloat(avgTimeCorrect.toFixed(1) || '0'),
          avgTimeIncorrect: parseFloat(avgTimeIncorrect.toFixed(1) || '0'),
          count: qtAttempts.length
        };
      })
      .filter(item => item.count > 5) // Only show if decent sample size
      .sort((a, b) => b.avgTime - a.avgTime) // Sort by overall average time
      .slice(0, 10); // Top 10 by time

    return {
      overall: [
        { name: 'LR Average', time: parseFloat(avgTimeLR.toFixed(1)) },
        { name: 'RC Average', time: parseFloat(avgTimeRC.toFixed(1)) },
      ],
      lrComparison: [
        { name: 'LR Correct', time: parseFloat(avgTimeCorrectLR.toFixed(1) || '0') },
        { name: 'LR Incorrect', time: parseFloat(avgTimeIncorrectLR.toFixed(1) || '0') },
      ],
      rcComparison: [
        { name: 'RC Correct', time: parseFloat(avgTimeCorrectRC.toFixed(1) || '0') },
        { name: 'RC Incorrect', time: parseFloat(avgTimeIncorrectRC.toFixed(1) || '0') },
      ],
      byQuestionType
    };
  }, [attempts]);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <MotivationalMessageDisplay message="Pacing is crucial on the LSAT. Understanding where your time goes can help you optimize your strategy. Aim for efficiency, not just speed." />
      
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
          <ChartContainer title="Avg. Time: LR vs RC (seconds)">
            <ResponsiveContainer>
              <BarChart data={timingData.overall} layout="vertical">
                <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" />
                <XAxis type="number" unit="s" />
                <YAxis dataKey="name" type="category" width={100}/>
                <Tooltip />
                <Bar dataKey="time" fill="#4A90E2" />
              </BarChart>
            </ResponsiveContainer>
          </ChartContainer>

          <ChartContainer title="Avg. Time: Correct vs Incorrect (seconds)">
             <ResponsiveContainer>
                <BarChart data={[...timingData.lrComparison, ...timingData.rcComparison]}>
                    <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" />
                    <XAxis dataKey="name" />
                    <YAxis unit="s" />
                    <Tooltip />
                    <Legend />
                    <Bar dataKey="time" name="Avg. Time (s)">
                        {timingData.lrComparison.map((entry, index) => (
                            <Cell key={`cell-lr-${index}`} fill={index % 2 === 0 ? '#82ca9d' : '#FA8072'} />
                        ))}
                         {timingData.rcComparison.map((entry, index) => (
                            <Cell key={`cell-rc-${index}`} fill={index % 2 === 0 ? '#8884d8' : '#FF8C69'} />
                        ))}
                    </Bar>
                </BarChart>
            </ResponsiveContainer>
          </ChartContainer>
      </div>

      <ChartContainer title="Avg. Time by Question Type (Top 10, seconds)">
        <ResponsiveContainer>
            <BarChart data={timingData.byQuestionType}>
                <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" />
                <XAxis dataKey="questionType" angle={-30} textAnchor="end" height={70} interval={0} />
                <YAxis />
                <Tooltip />
                <Legend />
                <Bar dataKey="avgTime" name="Avg. Time" fill="#FFC658" />
                <Bar dataKey="avgTimeCorrect" name="Avg. Correct" fill="#A4DE6C" />
                <Bar dataKey="avgTimeIncorrect" name="Avg. Incorrect" fill="#FF8042" />
            </BarChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer>
      </ChartContainer>
    </div>
  );
};
//endregion TimingAnalysisTab

//region RecentActivityFeed (used in OverallPerformanceTab)
//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
interface RecentActivityFeedProps {
  attempts: QuestionAttempt[]; // Expects a small number of recent attempts
}

const RecentActivityFeed: React.FC<RecentActivityFeedProps> = ({ attempts }) => {
  if (attempts.length === 0) {
    return (
      <Card title="Recent Activity">
        <p className="text-gray-500">No recent activity to display for this period.</p>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  return (
    <Card title="Recent Activity (Last 10 Questions)">
      <ul className="space-y-3">
        {attempts.map(attempt => (
          <li key={attempt.id} className="flex justify-between items-center p-3 border border-gray-200 rounded-md">
            <div>
              <span className="font-medium text-gray-800">{attempt.section} - {attempt.questionType}</span>
              <span className="block text-xs text-gray-500">
                {new Date(attempt.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString()} on {new Date(attempt.timestamp).toLocaleDateString()} | 
                Difficulty: {attempt.difficulty} | Time: {attempt.timeSpentSeconds}s
              </span>
            </div>
            <span className={`px-2 py-1 text-xs font-semibold rounded-full ${
              attempt.isCorrect ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 'bg-red-100 text-red-700'
            }`}>
              {attempt.isCorrect ? 'Correct' : 'Incorrect'}
            </span>
          </li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </Card>
  );
};

//endregion

//endregion UI Components

const AnalyticsDashboard: React.FC = () => {
  const [currentFilter, setCurrentFilter] = useState<TimeFilterOption>('all');
  const [allAttempts] = useState<QuestionAttempt[]>(ALL_MOCK_ATTEMPTS); // In real app, fetch this

  const filteredAttempts = useMemo(() => {
    return filterAttemptsByTime(allAttempts, currentFilter);
  }, [allAttempts, currentFilter]);

  useEffect(() => {
    // This is to simulate data changing slightly if needed, or just to ensure re-renders
    // In a real app, data fetching logic would go here or in a global state manager
    console.log(`Filter changed to: ${currentFilter}, ${filteredAttempts.length} attempts shown.`);
  }, [currentFilter, filteredAttempts]);

  return (
    <div className="analytics-dashboard p-4 md:p-8 bg-gray-100 min-h-screen font-sans">
      <header className="mb-8 text-center">
        <h1 className="text-4xl font-bold text-gray-800">Your LSAT Analytics</h1>
        <p className="text-lg text-gray-600">Track your progress, identify weaknesses, and conquer the LSAT!</p>
      </header>

      <TimeFilter selectedFilter={currentFilter} onFilterChange={setCurrentFilter} />

      {filteredAttempts.length === 0 && currentFilter !== 'all' ? (
        <Card title="No Data">
          <p className="text-gray-600 text-center py-8">
            No activity recorded for the selected period ({currentFilter}). Try a different time filter or complete some questions!
          </p>
          <MotivationalMessageDisplay message="Every master was once a beginner. Keep going!"/>
        </Card>
      ) : (
        <Tabs selectedTabClassName="border-b-2 !border-blue-600 !text-blue-600" className="mt-6">
          <TabList className="flex border-b border-gray-300 mb-6 react-tabs__tab-list">
            {['Overview', 'By Question Type', 'Difficulty & Logic', 'Timing Analysis'].map(label => (
              <Tab key={label} className="px-4 py-3 font-medium text-gray-600 hover:text-blue-600 cursor-pointer focus:outline-none react-tabs__tab">
                {label}
              </Tab>

          </TabList>

          <TabPanel className="react-tabs__tab-panel">
            <OverallPerformanceTab attempts={filteredAttempts} />
          </TabPanel>
          <TabPanel className="react-tabs__tab-panel">
            <QuestionTypeTab attempts={filteredAttempts} frequencies={MOCK_QUESTION_TYPE_FREQUENCIES} />
          </TabPanel>
          <TabPanel className="react-tabs__tab-panel">
            <DifficultyLogicTab attempts={filteredAttempts} drills={MOCK_DRILLS} />
          </TabPanel>
          <TabPanel className="react-tabs__tab-panel">
            <TimingAnalysisTab attempts={filteredAttempts} />
          </TabPanel>
        </Tabs>
      )}
      
      {/* Basic CSS for layout (can be replaced with Tailwind or other CSS solutions) */}
      <style jsx global>{`
        .analytics-dashboard { font-family: 'Inter', sans-serif; /* Example modern font */ }
        .time-filter-controls button { outline: none; }
        .time-filter-controls button:focus { box-shadow: 0 0 0 2px rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.5); } // Example focus ring
        
        /* react-tabs overrides/enhancements */
        .react-tabs__tab-list {
          margin: 0 0 1.5rem 0; /* 24px */
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          border-bottom: 1px solid #D1D5DB; /* gray-300 */
        }
        .react-tabs__tab {
          padding: 0.75rem 1rem; /* 12px 16px */
          font-weight: 500; /* medium */
          color: #4B5563; /* gray-600 */
          cursor: pointer;
          border: none; /* remove default borders */
          border-bottom: 2px solid transparent; /* for selected state */
          margin-bottom: -1px; /* align with bottom border of list */
          transition: color 0.2s ease, border-color 0.2s ease;
        }
        .react-tabs__tab:hover {
          color: #2563EB; /* blue-600 */
        }
        .react-tabs__tab--selected {
          color: #2563EB !important; /* blue-600 */
          border-bottom: 2px solid #2563EB !important; /* blue-600 */
          font-weight: 600; /* semibold */
        }
        .react-tabs__tab--disabled {
          color: #9CA3AF; /* gray-400 */
          cursor: default;
        }
        .react-tabs__tab:focus {
          outline: none;
          box-shadow: 0 0 0 2px rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3); /* blue-600 with opacity */
          border-radius: 4px; /* slight rounding on focus for visibility */
        }
        .react-tabs__tab-panel {
          display: none;
        }
        .react-tabs__tab-panel--selected {
          display: block;
        }

        /* Basic Grid (can be done with Tailwind classes directly) */
        .grid { display: grid; }
        .grid-cols-1 { grid-template-columns: repeat(1, minmax(0, 1fr)); }
        @media (min-width: 768px) { /* md breakpoint */
          .md\:grid-cols-2 { grid-template-columns: repeat(2, minmax(0, 1fr)); }
        }
        .gap-6 { gap: 1.5rem; } /* 24px */
        .space-y-6 > :not([hidden]) ~ :not([hidden]) { margin-top: 1.5rem; }
        .mb-6 { margin-bottom: 1.5rem; }
        .mb-8 { margin-bottom: 2rem; }
        .p-4 { padding: 1rem; }
        .md\:p-8 { padding: 2rem; }

      `}</style>
    </div>
  );
};

---

# old analytics

import React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { AgGridReact } from 'ag-grid-react';
import 'ag-grid-community/styles/ag-grid.css';
import 'ag-grid-community/styles/ag-theme-alpine.css';

export default function Analytics({ userInfo }) {
    const [selectedPrimaryFilter, setSelectedPrimaryFilter] = useState('tests'); // 'tests' or 'questions'
    const [selectedQuestionFilter, setSelectedQuestionFilter] = useState('all'); // 'all', 'type', 'category', 'difficulty'
    const [selectedQuestionDetail, setSelectedQuestionDetail] = useState(''); // e.g., specific type, category, or difficulty value
    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

    const [tests, setTests] = useState([]); // To store list of tests [{id: string, name: string}]
    const [questionTypes, setQuestionTypes] = useState([]); // [{value: string, label: string}]
    const [questionCategories, setQuestionCategories] = useState([]); // [{value: string, label: string}]
    const difficulties = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];

    const [rowData, setRowData] = useState([]);
    const [columnDefs, setColumnDefs] = useState([]);

    // Process userInfo data when it changes
    useEffect(() => {
        if (!userInfo) return;
        
        // Extract completed tests
        if (userInfo.completedTests) {
            const testList = Object.entries(userInfo.completedTests).map(([id, data]) => ({
                id,
                name: `PrepTest ${id.replace('LSAC', '')}`
            }));
            setTests(testList);
        }
        
        // Extract question types
        if (userInfo.completedQuestionsByType) {
            const types = Object.keys(userInfo.completedQuestionsByType).map(type => ({
                value: type,
                label: type
            }));
            setQuestionTypes(types);
        }
        
        // Set question categories
        if (userInfo.completedQuestionsByCategory) {
            const categories = Object.keys(userInfo.completedQuestionsByCategory).map(category => ({
                value: category,
                label: category === 'LR' ? 'Logical Reasoning' : 
                       category === 'RC' ? 'Reading Comprehension' : category
            }));
            setQuestionCategories(categories);
        }
    }, [userInfo]);

    // Update grid data based on selected filters
    const updateGridData = useCallback(() => {
        if (!userInfo) return;
        
        if (selectedPrimaryFilter === 'tests') {
            // Display test analytics
            const testData = [];
            
            Object.entries(userInfo.completedTests || {}).forEach(([testId, data]) => {
                // Calculate performance metrics
                const correctCount = Array.isArray(data.performance) 
                    ? data.performance.filter(result => result === true).length 
                    : 0;
                const totalCount = Array.isArray(data.performance) 
                    ? data.performance.length 
                    : 0;
                const correctPercentage = totalCount > 0 
                    ? Math.round((correctCount / totalCount) * 100) 
                    : 0;
                
                // Calculate time metrics
                const totalTime = Array.isArray(data.time) 
                    ? data.time.reduce((sum, time) => sum + (time || 0), 0) 
                    : 0;
                const avgTimePerQuestion = totalCount > 0 
                    ? Math.round((totalTime / totalCount) * 10) / 10 
                    : 0;
                
                // Format date
                const dateStr = data.dateCompleted 
                    ? new Date(data.dateCompleted).toLocaleDateString() 
                    : 'Unknown';
                
                testData.push({
                    id: testId,
                    name: `PrepTest ${testId.replace('LSAC', '')}`,
                    date: dateStr,
                    score: `${correctCount}/${totalCount}`,
                    percentage: correctPercentage + '%',
                    totalTime: formatTime(totalTime),
                    avgTimePerQuestion: avgTimePerQuestion + 's'
                });
            });
            
            setRowData(testData);
            setColumnDefs([
                { field: 'name', headerName: 'Test Name', sortable: true, filter: true },
                { field: 'date', headerName: 'Completed On', sortable: true },
                { field: 'score', headerName: 'Score', sortable: true },
                { field: 'percentage', headerName: 'Percentage', sortable: true },
                { field: 'totalTime', headerName: 'Total Time', sortable: true },
                { field: 'avgTimePerQuestion', headerName: 'Avg Time per Question', sortable: true }
            ]);
        } else if (selectedPrimaryFilter === 'questions') {
            // Display question analytics based on filters
            let questionData = [];
            
            if (selectedQuestionFilter === 'all') {
                // Aggregate all questions
                Object.entries(userInfo.completedQuestions || {}).forEach(([questionId, data]) => {
                    if (data.completed) {
                        questionData.push({
                            id: questionId,
                            type: data.type || 'Unknown',
                            category: data.category || 'Unknown',
                            difficulty: data.difficulty || 'Unknown',
                            correct: data.isRight ? 'Yes' : 'No',
                            test: data.testId || 'Unknown',
                            dateCompleted: data.dateCompleted ? new Date(data.dateCompleted).toLocaleDateString() : 'Unknown'
                        });
                    }
                });
            } else if (selectedQuestionFilter === 'type' && selectedQuestionDetail) {
                // Filter by question type
                Object.entries(userInfo.completedQuestions || {}).forEach(([questionId, data]) => {
                    if (data.completed && data.type === selectedQuestionDetail) {
                        questionData.push({
                            id: questionId,
                            category: data.category || 'Unknown',
                            difficulty: data.difficulty || 'Unknown',
                            correct: data.isRight ? 'Yes' : 'No',
                            test: data.testId || 'Unknown',
                            dateCompleted: data.dateCompleted ? new Date(data.dateCompleted).toLocaleDateString() : 'Unknown'
                        });
                    }
                });
            } else if (selectedQuestionFilter === 'category' && selectedQuestionDetail) {
                // Filter by question category
                Object.entries(userInfo.completedQuestions || {}).forEach(([questionId, data]) => {
                    if (data.completed && data.category === selectedQuestionDetail) {
                        questionData.push({
                            id: questionId,
                            type: data.type || 'Unknown',
                            difficulty: data.difficulty || 'Unknown',
                            correct: data.isRight ? 'Yes' : 'No',
                            test: data.testId || 'Unknown',
                            dateCompleted: data.dateCompleted ? new Date(data.dateCompleted).toLocaleDateString() : 'Unknown'
                        });
                    }
                });
            } else if (selectedQuestionFilter === 'difficulty' && selectedQuestionDetail) {
                // Filter by difficulty
                Object.entries(userInfo.completedQuestions || {}).forEach(([questionId, data]) => {
                    if (data.completed && data.difficulty == selectedQuestionDetail) {
                        questionData.push({
                            id: questionId,
                            type: data.type || 'Unknown',
                            category: data.category || 'Unknown',
                            correct: data.isRight ? 'Yes' : 'No',
                            test: data.testId || 'Unknown',
                            dateCompleted: data.dateCompleted ? new Date(data.dateCompleted).toLocaleDateString() : 'Unknown'
                        });
                    }
                });
            }
            
            const baseColumns = [
                { field: 'id', headerName: 'Question ID', sortable: true, filter: true },
                { field: 'correct', headerName: 'Correct', sortable: true, filter: true },
                { field: 'test', headerName: 'Test', sortable: true, filter: true },
                { field: 'dateCompleted', headerName: 'Date Completed', sortable: true }
            ];
            
            // Conditionally add columns based on the filter
            const columns = [...baseColumns];
            if (selectedQuestionFilter !== 'type') {
                columns.splice(1, 0, { field: 'type', headerName: 'Question Type', sortable: true, filter: true });
            }
            if (selectedQuestionFilter !== 'category') {
                columns.splice(selectedQuestionFilter === 'type' ? 1 : 2, 0, 
                    { field: 'category', headerName: 'Category', sortable: true, filter: true });
            }
            if (selectedQuestionFilter !== 'difficulty') {
                columns.splice(columns.length - 2, 0, 
                    { field: 'difficulty', headerName: 'Difficulty', sortable: true, filter: true });
            }
            
            setRowData(questionData);
            setColumnDefs(columns);
        }
    }, [selectedPrimaryFilter, selectedQuestionFilter, selectedQuestionDetail, userInfo]);

    useEffect(() => {
        updateGridData();
    }, [updateGridData]);

    // Format seconds into MM:SS
    const formatTime = (seconds) => {
        if (!seconds && seconds !== 0) return 'N/A';
        const mins = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
        const secs = Math.floor(seconds % 60);
        return `${mins}:${secs.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
    };

    const commonSelectClass = "block w-full p-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md shadow-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500 focus:border-indigo-500 bg-white text-gray-700 hover:border-gray-400";

    const handlePrimaryFilterChange = (e) => {
        const newFilter = e.target.value;
        setSelectedPrimaryFilter(newFilter);
        setSelectedQuestionFilter('all'); 
        setSelectedQuestionDetail('');
    };

    const handleQuestionFilterChange = (e) => {
        setSelectedQuestionFilter(e.target.value);
        setSelectedQuestionDetail(''); 
    };

    // Display a loading state if data is still being fetched
    if (loading) {
        return (
            <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-lg p-6">
                <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-800 mb-6">Analytics</h2>
                <div className="flex justify-center items-center h-64">
                    <p className="text-gray-500">Loading analytics data...</p>
                </div>
            </div>
        );
    }

    // Display message if userInfo is not available
    if (!userInfo) {
        return (
            <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-lg p-6">
                <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-800 mb-6">Analytics</h2>
                <div className="flex justify-center items-center h-64">
                    <p className="text-gray-500">Unable to load user data. Please try refreshing the page.</p>
                </div>
            </div>
        );
    }

    return (
        <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-lg p-6">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-800 mb-6">Analytics</h2>

            {/* Unified Filter Row */}
            <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:space-x-4 mb-6 sm:items-end">
                {/* Primary Filter */}
                <div className="w-full sm:flex-1 sm:min-w-0 sm:max-w-xs">
                    <label htmlFor="primaryFilter" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">View Analytics For:</label>
                    <select
                        id="primaryFilter"
                        value={selectedPrimaryFilter}
                        onChange={handlePrimaryFilterChange}
                        className={commonSelectClass}
                    >
                        <option value="tests">Tests</option>
                        <option value="questions">Questions</option>
                    </select>
                </div>

                {/* Question Filter Type (conditionally shown) */}
                {selectedPrimaryFilter === 'questions' && (
                    <div className="w-full sm:flex-1 sm:min-w-0 sm:max-w-xs mt-4 sm:mt-0">
                        <label htmlFor="questionFilterType" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Filter Questions By:</label>
                        <select
                            id="questionFilterType"
                            value={selectedQuestionFilter}
                            onChange={handleQuestionFilterChange}
                            className={commonSelectClass}
                        >
                            <option value="all">All Questions</option>
                            <option value="type">By Type</option>
                            <option value="category">By Category</option>
                            <option value="difficulty">By Difficulty</option>
                        </select>
                    </div>
                )}

                {/* Question Detail Filter (conditionally shown) */}
                {selectedPrimaryFilter === 'questions' && selectedQuestionFilter !== 'all' && (
                    <div className="w-full sm:flex-1 sm:min-w-0 sm:max-w-xs mt-4 sm:mt-0 relative">
                        {selectedQuestionFilter === 'type' && (
                            <>
                                <label htmlFor="typeDetail" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Select Type:</label>
                                <select
                                    id="typeDetail"
                                    value={selectedQuestionDetail}
                                    onChange={(e) => setSelectedQuestionDetail(e.target.value)}
                                    className={commonSelectClass}
                                    disabled={!questionTypes.length}
                                >
                                    <option value="">-- Select Type --</option>
                                    {questionTypes.map(type => <option key={type.value} value={type.value}>{type.label}</option>)}
                                </select>
                            </>
                        )}
                        {selectedQuestionFilter === 'category' && (
                            <>
                                <label htmlFor="categoryDetail" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Select Category:</label>
                                <select
                                    id="categoryDetail"
                                    value={selectedQuestionDetail}
                                    onChange={(e) => setSelectedQuestionDetail(e.target.value)}
                                    className={commonSelectClass}
                                    disabled={!questionCategories.length}
                                >
                                    <option value="">-- Select Category --</option>
                                    {questionCategories.map(cat => <option key={cat.value} value={cat.value}>{cat.label}</option>)}
                                </select>
                            </>
                        )}
                        {selectedQuestionFilter === 'difficulty' && (
                            <>
                                <label htmlFor="difficultyDetail" className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Select Difficulty:</label>
                                <select
                                    id="difficultyDetail"
                                    value={selectedQuestionDetail}
                                    onChange={(e) => setSelectedQuestionDetail(e.target.value)}
                                    className={commonSelectClass}
                                >
                                    <option value="">-- Select Difficulty --</option>
                                    {difficulties.map(d => <option key={d} value={d}>{d}</option>)}
                                </select>
                            </>
                        )}
                        {/* Message area positioned absolutely to prevent layout shift */}
                        {(!selectedQuestionDetail && (selectedQuestionFilter === 'type' || selectedQuestionFilter === 'category' || selectedQuestionFilter === 'difficulty')) && (
                            <div className="absolute bottom-[-1em] left-0 w-full">
                                <p className="pt-1 text-xs text-gray-500">
                                    Please select a specific {selectedQuestionFilter}.
                                </p>
                            </div>
                        )}
                    </div>
                )}
            </div>

            {/* No data message */}
            {rowData.length === 0 && (
                <div className="mt-6 p-4 border border-gray-200 rounded-lg">
                    <p className="text-gray-600 text-center">
                        {selectedPrimaryFilter === 'tests' 
                            ? "No test data available. Complete tests to see analytics." 
                            : selectedQuestionFilter === 'all'
                                ? "No question data available. Complete questions to see analytics."
                                : `No ${selectedQuestionFilter === 'type' 
                                    ? selectedQuestionDetail 
                                    : selectedQuestionFilter === 'category'
                                        ? selectedQuestionDetail
                                        : `difficulty ${selectedQuestionDetail}`} questions completed yet.`}
                    </p>
                </div>
            )}

            {/* AG Grid Table */}
            {rowData.length > 0 && (
                <div className="ag-theme-alpine mt-6" style={{ height: 600, width: '100%' }}>
                    <AgGridReact
                        rowData={rowData}
                        columnDefs={columnDefs}
                        domLayout='autoHeight'
                        pagination={true}
                        paginationPageSize={10}
                        defaultColDef={{
                            flex: 1,
                            minWidth: 100,
                            resizable: true
                        }}
                    />
                </div>
            )}

            {/* Analytics Summary (shown when data is available) */}
            {rowData.length > 0 && (
                <div className="mt-6">
                    <h3 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-800 mb-2">Summary</h3>
                    {selectedPrimaryFilter === 'tests' && (
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                            <div className="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg">
                                <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Total Tests Completed</p>
                                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-800">{rowData.length}</p>
                            </div>
                            <div className="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg">
                                <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Average Score</p>
                                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-800">
                                    {Math.round(rowData.reduce((sum, test) => {
                                        const percentage = parseInt(test.percentage, 10) || 0;
                                        return sum + percentage;
                                    }, 0) / rowData.length)}%
                                </p>
                            </div>
                            <div className="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg">
                                <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Most Recent Test</p>
                                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-800">
                                    {rowData.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date) - new Date(a.date))[0]?.name || 'N/A'}
                                </p>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    )}
                    {selectedPrimaryFilter === 'questions' && (
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                            <div className="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg">
                                <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Total Questions Answered</p>
                                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-800">{rowData.length}</p>
                            </div>
                            <div className="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg">
                                <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Correct Answers</p>
                                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-800">
                                    {rowData.filter(q => q.correct === 'Yes').length} 
                                    ({Math.round((rowData.filter(q => q.correct === 'Yes').length / rowData.length) * 100)}%)
                                </p>
                            </div>
                            <div className="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg">
                                <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Most Recent Question</p>
                                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-800">
                                    {rowData.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.dateCompleted) - new Date(a.dateCompleted))[0]?.id || 'N/A'}
                                </p>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    )}
                </div>
            )}
        </div>
    );
}

---

# New rules

# Cursor IDE Contribution Guidelines

> **Purpose** – A living playbook for *how* we build inside Cursor IDE: coding standards, reproducible environments, AI guard‑rails, testing, performance, security, and communication norms. It complements any language‑specific style guides and automated linters.

---

## 📑 Table of Contents

1. [Workflow Fundamentals](#workflow-fundamentals)
2. [Code Quality & Safety](#code-quality--safety)
3. [Architecture & UI Structure](#architecture--ui-structure)
4. [Environment Management](#environment-management)
5. [Issue Resolution & Debugging](#issue-resolution--debugging)
6. [Performance, Accessibility & Quality Gates](#performance-accessibility--quality-gates)
7. [Documentation & Persistent Logs](#documentation--persistent-logs)
8. [Cursor IDE & AI Guard‑Rails](#cursor-ide--ai-guard-rails)
9. [Testing & Continuous Integration](#testing--continuous-integration)
10. [Security Enhancements](#security-enhancements)
11. [Team Enablement & On‑boarding](#team-enablement--on-boarding)
12. [Monitoring & Observability](#monitoring--observability)
13. [Platform Compatibility](#platform-compatibility)
14. [Communication Protocols](#communication-protocols)
15. [Snapshot Checklist](#snapshot-checklist)

---

## Workflow Fundamentals

> **What is a Cursor snapshot?** A snapshot is a lightweight save‑point inside Cursor IDE that captures the entire workspace state along with a commit‑style message. Create one at every logical milestone so you can diff, branch, or roll back without leaving Cursor.

| # | Convention                                                                                            | Rationale                |
| - | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------ |
| 1 | **Interrogate the task.** Clarify until goal & success criteria are clear.                            | Avoid wasted cycles.     |
| 2 | **Reflect Next Steps.** End every update with a bullet list of upcoming actions.                      | Keeps momentum.          |
| 3 | **Single‑topic snapshots.** Save frequent, descriptive Cursor snapshots to enable rollback & diffing. | Lightweight versioning.  |
| 4 | **Windows‑first.** PowerShell examples, back‑slash paths, CRLF endings.                               | Matches deployment host. |

> *Optional Git*: If using Git, snapshot first, then `git commit` with the same message. Branch prefixes: `feature/`, `bugfix/`, `hotfix/`; follow Conventional Commits (`feat:`, `fix:`, `docs:`).

---

## Code Quality & Safety

1. **Explicit error handling.** Surface actionable messages; no silent failures.
2. **Ban deprecated / insecure APIs.** Add offenders to **`DEPRECATED.txt`** with migration notes.
3. **Dependency discipline.** Prefer std‑lib or approved packages; new ones require review & **`DEPENDENCIES.md`** entry.
4. **Import order.** Standard‑lib ➔ third‑party ➔ internal modules.
5. **Comment intent, not mechanics.** Explain *why* complex logic exists.
6. **Static analysis gate.** ESLint / Pylint / MyPy / TypeScript strict must be green.

---

## Architecture & UI Structure

### File Organisation & Component Architecture

* **Mirror ********`STRUCTURE.md`********.** Consult the directory map **before** creating new modules to understand where they belong, and update the map whenever you add, move, or delete files..\*\*  Any file you add, move, or delete **must** be reflected in the directory map.
* **Atomic design hierarchy** – organise components as:

  ```
  atoms/       # Button, Input, Icon
  molecules/   # SearchBox, Card
  organisms/   # Header, DataTable, ProductGrid
  templates/   # DashboardLayout, MarketingLayout
  pages/       # HomePage, SettingsPage
  ```
* **Modular UI.**  Pages/layouts, components, graphs, and styles live in separate files and are composed, not nested monoliths.
* **Global styles first.**  Extend shared style sheets before inventing new ones to enforce consistency.

---

### 🎨 Design Philosophy

| Principle                      | Implementation                                        | Example                                          |
| ------------------------------ | ----------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------ |
| **Attractive & Sophisticated** | Modern patterns, subtle motion, professional palettes | Card shadows @4dp, soft gradients                |
| **Simplicity over Complexity** | Progressive disclosure, clear hierarchy               | Hide advanced filters behind «More» toggle       |
| **Consistency**                | Design tokens & reusable components                   | Same primary button across app                   |
| **Performance‑First**          | Optimised images & transforms‑only animations         | `loading="lazy"`, CSS `transform: translateZ(0)` |

---

### 📱 Responsive Design Strategy

Breakpoints (mobile‑first): `xs <640`, `sm ≥640`, `md ≥768`, `lg ≥1024`, `xl ≥1280`, `2xl ≥1536` px.

| Device Class       | Key Rules                           | Implementation                    |
| ------------------ | ----------------------------------- | --------------------------------- |
| **Mobile (xs/sm)** | Thumb ergonomics & priority content | ≥ 44 px touch targets, bottom nav |
| **Tablet (md)**    | Hybrid input & reading comfort      | Sidebar + spacious grids          |
| **Desktop (lg+)**  | Dense data & power features         | Hover states, keyboard shortcuts  |

All components **must** degrade gracefully and pass Chrome DevTools’ responsive checker.

---

### 🏗️ Application‑Type Playbooks

* **Dashboards** – Sidebar nav + widget grid, Recharts for viz, skeleton loaders, virtual tables.
* **Marketing Sites** – Hero ➔ features ➔ social proof ➔ CTA.  High‑impact media with reduced‑motion fallback.
* **SaaS Apps** – Progressive onboarding, persistent primary nav, real‑time data, logical settings groups.
* **E‑commerce** – Variant pickers, zoomable images, persistent cart, guest checkout.

---

### 🧩 Component Requirements Matrix

| Component           | Must Have               | Should Have          | Nice to Have            |
| ------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------- | ----------------------- |
| **Buttons / Links** | Focus & disabled states | Keyboard shortcuts   | Micro‑animations        |
| **Tables**          | Sort & paginate         | Column filter/export | Virtual scroll          |
| **Forms**           | Validation & errors     | Autosave             | Progressive enhancement |
| **Navigation**      | Active state            | Breadcrumbs          | Recent items            |

---

### 🎨 Visual Design System

* **Color tokens** – semantic variables (`--color-primary`, `--color-error`) defined in CSS‑vars, with WCAG AA 4.5:1 contrast.
* **Dark mode** – Same tokens re‑mapped; toggle persists preference; respect `prefers-color-scheme`.
* **Fluid type scale** – Clamp‑based sizing from `text-xs` → `text-6xl`; 1.5 line‑height; 65 ch max width.

---

### ♿ Accessibility Standards

* **WCAG 2.1 AA baseline** – Keyboard nav, alt text, focus rings, contrast.
* Respect `prefers-reduced-motion`; animations disabled if true.
* Use semantic HTML and ARIA where required; run `npm run a11y` (axe‑core) before snapshot.

---

### ⚡ Performance Targets

| Metric  | Target   |
| ------- | -------- |
| **FCP** | < 1.5 s  |
| **LCP** | < 2.5 s  |
| **CLS** | < 0.1    |
| **INP** | < 200 ms |

**Optimisation checklist:** WebP + lazy images, `font-display: swap`, code‑splitting, critical CSS inline.

---

### ✨ Animation & Interaction Rules

* **Purpose‑driven** – no gratuitous motion.
* **Duration** – 200‑300 ms micro, 300‑500 ms transitions.
* **Properties** – Only `transform` & `opacity` animated; avoid layout‑thrashing.

```css
.interactive:hover { transform: translateY(-2px); }
.interactive:active { transform: translateY(0); }
.loading { pointer-events:none; }
```

---

### ✅ Quality Gates

* **Visual regression** – Playwright screenshot diffs on lg & xs breakpoints.
* **Automated a11y** – axe-core CI must score ≥ 90.
* **Bundle budget** – Fail build if main chunk > 250 kB gzip or +15 %.

---

## Environment Management Management

Environment drift is the #1 “works‑on‑my‑machine” culprit. All work **must** happen inside a pinned environment.

### Conda‑First Flow

| # | Rule                                                                                 | Command / File                                 |
| - | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ---------------------------------------------- |
| 1 | **Per‑project env.** `.conda/<project>‑py<maj>‑gpu`.                                 | `conda create -n myproj-py311-gpu python=3.11` |
| 2 | **CPU & CUDA YAMLs.** Separate files: `environment.yml`, `environment.cuda118.yml` … |                                                |
| 3 | **Lock it.** `conda-lock lock --mamba -f environment.yml` → `conda-lock.yml`.        |                                                |
| 4 | **direnv auto‑activation.** `.envrc` setup.                                          |                                                |
| 5 | **pip‑tools fallback.** Only for packages absent from Conda.                         |                                                |

Dev‑container parity: `.devcontainer/Dockerfile` mirrors the env so CI & Codespaces run identical stacks.

Run `make env-check` before each snapshot; CI echoes the same.

---

## Issue Resolution & Debugging

| Step | Checklist                                                                                                                      |
| ---- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| 1    | **Verify env.** `conda list` vs `conda-lock.yml`.                                                                              |
| 2    | **Lint.** Run static analysers.                                                                                                |
| 3    | **Dependency diff.** Check for version mismatches.                                                                             |
| 4    | **Rollback test.** Reproduce on previous snapshot.                                                                             |
| 5    | **Escalate.** If blocked >2 hrs → add entry to **`PROBLEM_LOG.txt`** (timestamp, owner, summary) and ping the support channel. |

---

## Performance, Accessibility & Quality Gates

| Category            | Standard                                                                       | Tooling                                               |
| ------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | ----------------------------------------------------- |
| **Bundle size**     | Fail build if main bundle >250 kB or +15 % vs previous.                        | `vite-bundle-visualizer` / `webpack-bundle-analyzer`. |
| **Core Web Vitals** | LCP ≤ 2.5 s, CLS ≤ 0.1, INP ≤ 200 ms.                                          | Lighthouse CI.                                        |
| **Accessibility**   | WCAG 2.1 AA.                                                                   | `axe-core` in CI.                                     |
| **Browser matrix**  | Latest Edge/Chrome/Firefox, Safari 14+, and Chromium‑based WebView on Windows. | Playwright tests.                                     |

---

## Documentation & Persistent Logs

| File              | Purpose                                                                                                               |
| ----------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `README.md`       | Setup, run, test, deploy – copy‑pastable commands.                                                                    |
| `STRUCTURE.md`    | Directory map and boundaries.                                                                                         |
| `DEPRECATED.txt`  | ❌ Forbidden patterns.                                                                                                 |
| `PROBLEM_LOG.txt` | Persistent blockers diary.                                                                                            |
| `ENVIRONMENTS.md` | List of env YAMLs & CUDA/Python matrices.                                                                             |
| `DEPENDENCIES.md` | Rationale & licence notes for third‑party libs not pinned by the Conda lock (pip‑tools extras, external services).    |
| `CHANGELOG.md`    | Auto‑generated log of user‑visible changes (*built via ****`npm run changelog`****, which parses snapshot messages*). |

> **Rule of Two Reads** – Open core docs **before** starting work **and** before snapshotting; update them if anything changed.

---

## Cursor IDE & AI Guard‑Rails

1. **Tag context.** Prefix complex requests with `@Files`, `@Code`, `@Docs` lists.
2. **Incremental prompts.** Break large changes into small, verifiable steps.
3. **Iterate on lints.** Enable *Iterate on Lints*; AI must satisfy static analysers.
4. **Human review gates.** Security‑sensitive, performance‑critical, or architectural changes require manual inspect.
5. **Prompt library.** Keep `prompts/` folder with reusable good prompts.

---

## Testing & Continuous Integration

* **TDD encouraged.** Write failing test first.
* **Windows CI** steps: env → lint → test → a11y → perf budgets → build.
* **Coverage floor:** 80 % lines & branches.
* **Accessibility & Perf budgets** enforced in pipeline.

---

## Security Enhancements

* **Dependency scanning.** `npm audit`, `pip-audit`, or `conda‑tree` in CI.
* **Environment isolation.** No prod secrets in dev envs; secrets via `.env` templates.
* **Access logging.** Enable workspace activity logs.
* **Secret scanning hooks.** Pre‑save hooks reject AWS/GCP keys.

---

## Team Enablement & On‑boarding

| Phase     | Activity                                                              |
| --------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Day 0     | Install Conda, enable direnv, run `make env-create`, run sample test. |
| Week 1    | Pair programming on a low‑risk task; demo snapshot workflow.          |
| Ongoing   | Weekly “Show & Tell” demo of new features or lessons learned.         |
| Quarterly | Review guidelines; tag & tackle documentation debt.                   |

---

## Monitoring & Observability

* **Structured logging** with correlation IDs.
* **Error tracking** – Sentry or equivalent; alerts in MS Teams.
* **Real user monitoring** – Web‑Vitals emission.
* **Synthetic uptime checks** – Ping health endpoint every 1 min.
* **One‑click rollback** – Via deployment script; health verified post‑rollback.

---

## Platform Compatibility

* Use `path.join()` or similar abstractions.
* Test matrix covers Windows 10/11, WSL2 Ubuntu, and latest macOS.
* Configure editors to respect `.editorconfig` for mixed line endings.

---

## Communication Protocols

* Address the owner as **“Jack”** in chat and snapshot comments.
* End every message with a **Next Steps** block.
* Only change an existing **Next Steps** section if scope shifts.
