# chart example

"use client"

import { useState, useRef } from "react"
import { Area, AreaChart, ResponsiveContainer, Tooltip } from "@/components/ui/chart"
import { Card } from "@/components/ui/card"

// Platform advantages data - 4 key points
const advantages = [
  {
    id: 1,
    title: "Seamless Integration",
    description: "Our platform integrates effortlessly with your existing tools and workflows.",
    icon: "🔄",
  },
  {
    id: 2,
    title: "Real-time Analytics",
    description: "Get instant insights with powerful real-time data analytics and visualization.",
    icon: "📊",
  },
  {
    id: 3,
    title: "Advanced Security",
    description: "Enterprise-grade security with end-to-end encryption and compliance features.",
    icon: "🔒",
  },
  {
    id: 4,
    title: "Scalable Infrastructure",
    description: "Easily scale your operations as your business grows without performance issues.",
    icon: "📈",
  },
]

// Generate data points that will create a smooth curve through our advantage points
const generateCurveData = () => {
  // Define the exact positions where we want our advantage points
  const keyPoints = [
    { x: 5, y: 60 }, // First point - starts high
    { x: 33, y: 25 }, // Second point - dips low
    { x: 67, y: 55 }, // Third point - rises again
    { x: 95, y: 75 }, // Fourth point - ends higher
  ]

  const points = 100
  const data = []

  // Create a smooth curve that passes through our key points
  for (let i = 0; i < points; i++) {
    const x = i

    // Find the two closest key points
    let leftPoint = keyPoints[0]
    let rightPoint = keyPoints[keyPoints.length - 1]

    for (let j = 0; j < keyPoints.length - 1; j++) {
      if (x >= keyPoints[j].x && x <= keyPoints[j + 1].x) {
        leftPoint = keyPoints[j]
        rightPoint = keyPoints[j + 1]
        break
      }
    }

    // If we're at a key point, use its exact value
    if (keyPoints.some((point) => point.x === x)) {
      const keyPoint = keyPoints.find((point) => point.x === x)
      data.push({ x, y: keyPoint.y })
      continue
    }

    // Otherwise, interpolate between the two closest key points using a cubic function
    // for a smoother curve than linear interpolation
    const t = (x - leftPoint.x) / (rightPoint.x - leftPoint.x)

    // Cubic interpolation for smoother curves
    const t2 = t * t
    const t3 = t2 * t
    const h00 = 2 * t3 - 3 * t2 + 1
    const h10 = t3 - 2 * t2 + t
    const h01 = -2 * t3 + 3 * t2
    const h11 = t3 - t2

    // Tangent values for smooth curve
    const m0 = 0
    const m1 = 0

    // Calculate y value using cubic Hermite interpolation
    const y = h00 * leftPoint.y + h10 * m0 + h01 * rightPoint.y + h11 * m1

    // Add some small random variation for a more natural look
    const smallVariation = Math.sin(x * 0.3) * 2

    data.push({ x, y: y + smallVariation })
  }

  return data
}

// Extract the advantage points from the curve data
const extractAdvantagePoints = (curveData) => {
  const positions = [5, 33, 67, 95]

  return positions.map((pos, index) => ({
    ...advantages[index],
    x: pos,
    y: curveData[pos].y,
  }))
}

export function AdvantageGraph() {
  const [curveData] = useState(generateCurveData())
  const [advantagePoints] = useState(extractAdvantagePoints(curveData))
  const [activeAdvantage, setActiveAdvantage] = useState<number | null>(null)
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  // Create the data format expected by Recharts
  const chartData = curveData.map((point) => ({
    x: point.x,
    value: point.y,
    secondaryValue: point.y * 0.6 - 10, // For the secondary line
  }))

  // Create data specifically for the advantage points
  const pointsData = advantagePoints.map((point) => ({
    x: point.x,
    value: point.y,
  }))

  return (
    <div className="relative" ref={containerRef}>
      <div className="h-[400px] w-full">
        <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="100%">
          <AreaChart data={chartData} margin={{ top: 20, right: 20, left: 20, bottom: 20 }}>
            <defs>
              <linearGradient id="primaryGradient" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#f97316" stopOpacity={0.8} />
                <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#f97316" stopOpacity={0} />
              </linearGradient>
              <linearGradient id="secondaryGradient" x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#475569" stopOpacity={0.5} />
                <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#475569" stopOpacity={0} />
              </linearGradient>
            </defs>

            {/* Secondary area (dotted line in background) */}
            <Area
              type="monotone"
              dataKey="secondaryValue"
              stroke="#475569"
              strokeWidth={1}
              strokeDasharray="3 3"
              fill="url(#secondaryGradient)"
              isAnimationActive={true}
            />

            {/* Primary area (main orange line) */}
            <Area
              type="monotone"
              dataKey="value"
              stroke="#f97316"
              strokeWidth={3}
              fill="url(#primaryGradient)"
              isAnimationActive={true}
              activeDot={false} // We'll handle our own dots
            />

            {/* Custom tooltip that won't be shown - we'll use our own */}
            <Tooltip content={() => null} />
          </AreaChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer>
      </div>

      {/* Custom advantage points */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none" style={{ zIndex: 2 }}>
        {advantagePoints.map((point) => {
          // Calculate position based on the chart dimensions
          const xPos = `${(point.x / 100) * 100}%`
          const yPos = `${100 - ((point.y - 10) / 80) * 100}%`

          return (
            <div
              key={point.id}
              className="absolute -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 pointer-events-auto"
              style={{ left: xPos, top: yPos }}
              onMouseEnter={() => setActiveAdvantage(point.id)}
              onMouseLeave={() => setActiveAdvantage(null)}
            >
              <div
                className={`flex h-5 w-5 items-center justify-center rounded-full border-2 border-black bg-orange-500 transition-all duration-300 ${
                  activeAdvantage === point.id ? "scale-150 ring-4 ring-orange-300/30" : "hover:scale-125"
                }`}
              >
                <div className="h-1 w-1 rounded-full bg-black"></div>
              </div>

              {/* Tooltip */}
              {activeAdvantage === point.id && (
                <Card className="absolute z-10 w-64 bg-gray-800 text-white border-gray-700 shadow-xl -translate-x-1/2 p-3 mt-2">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                    <span className="text-xl">{point.icon}</span>
                    <h3 className="font-bold">{point.title}</h3>
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-sm text-gray-300">{point.description}</p>
                </Card>
              )}
            </div>
          )
        })}
      </div>

      {/* Mobile-friendly advantage list */}
      <div className="mt-8 md:hidden">
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white mb-4">Platform Advantages</h3>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4">
          {advantages.map((advantage) => (
            <Card key={advantage.id} className="bg-gray-800 text-white border-gray-700">
              <div className="p-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                  <span className="text-xl">{advantage.icon}</span>
                  <h4 className="font-bold">{advantage.title}</h4>
                </div>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-300">{advantage.description}</p>
              </div>
            </Card>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

# New who is voxhead for section

"use client"

import { useState, useEffect } from "react"
import Image from "next/image"
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion"
import { Brain, Wrench, Lightbulb, ArrowRight } from "lucide-react"
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button"

export default function WhoIsVoxHeadForMinimal1() {
  const [activeIndex, setActiveIndex] = useState(0)
  const [animationProgress, setAnimationProgress] = useState(0)

  const categories = [
    {
      id: "researchers",
      title: "Researchers & Academics",
      icon: <Brain className="h-6 w-6" />,
      description:
        "Students and researchers working in robotics, AI, human-robot interaction (HRI), embodied cognition, multimodal interfaces, or social robotics.",
      color: "#10b981", // emerald-500
      textColor: "text-emerald-500",
      borderColor: "border-emerald-500",
      bgColor: "bg-emerald-500",
      keywords: ["Robotics", "AI", "HRI", "Cognition", "Interfaces"],
    },
    {
      id: "makers",
      title: "Makers & Hobbyists",
      icon: <Wrench className="h-6 w-6" />,
      description: "Makers and hobbyists wanting to experiment with expressive, life-sized robots.",
      color: "#06b6d4", // cyan-500
      textColor: "text-cyan-500",
      borderColor: "border-cyan-500",
      bgColor: "bg-cyan-500",
      keywords: ["DIY", "3D Printing", "Electronics", "Prototyping", "Open Source"],
    },
    {
      id: "entrepreneurs",
      title: "Entrepreneurs & Innovators",
      icon: <Lightbulb className="h-6 w-6" />,
      description: "Entrepreneurs exploring robotic platforms for assistive tech, kiosks, or interaction design.",
      color: "#8b5cf6", // violet-500
      textColor: "text-violet-500",
      borderColor: "border-violet-500",
      bgColor: "bg-violet-500",
      keywords: ["Startups", "Innovation", "Assistive Tech", "Kiosks", "Interaction"],
    },
  ]

  // Auto-rotate through categories
  useEffect(() => {
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      setActiveIndex((prev) => (prev + 1) % categories.length)
    }, 8000)
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [categories.length])

  // Animation progress for circuit lines
  useEffect(() => {
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      setAnimationProgress((prev) => (prev + 0.01) % 1)
    }, 50)
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [])

  return (
    <section className="relative h-screen w-full overflow-hidden bg-gray-950">
      {/* Subtle grid background */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 z-0">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[linear-gradient(to_right,rgba(16,24,39,0.8),rgba(16,24,39,0.5))]"></div>
        <svg className="absolute h-full w-full opacity-5" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
          {/* Horizontal lines */}
          {Array.from({ length: 20 }).map((_, i) => (
            <line
              key={`h-${i}`}
              x1="0"
              y1={`${(i + 1) * 5}%`}
              x2="100%"
              y2={`${(i + 1) * 5}%`}
              stroke="#ffffff"
              strokeWidth="1"
            />
          ))}

          {/* Vertical lines */}
          {Array.from({ length: 20 }).map((_, i) => (
            <line
              key={`v-${i}`}
              x1={`${(i + 1) * 5}%`}
              y1="0"
              x2={`${(i + 1) * 5}%`}
              y2="100%"
              stroke="#ffffff"
              strokeWidth="1"
            />
          ))}
        </svg>

        {/* Subtle animated circuit lines */}
        <svg className="absolute h-full w-full opacity-10" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
          <defs>
            <linearGradient id="gradient1" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
              <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#10b981" stopOpacity="1" />
              <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#10b981" stopOpacity="0" />
            </linearGradient>
            <linearGradient id="gradient2" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
              <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#06b6d4" stopOpacity="1" />
              <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#06b6d4" stopOpacity="0" />
            </linearGradient>
            <linearGradient id="gradient3" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
              <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#8b5cf6" stopOpacity="1" />
              <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#8b5cf6" stopOpacity="0" />
            </linearGradient>
          </defs>

          {/* A few strategic circuit lines */}
          <line
            x1="0"
            y1="30%"
            x2="100%"
            y2="30%"
            stroke="url(#gradient1)"
            strokeWidth="1"
            strokeDasharray="10,15"
            strokeDashoffset={animationProgress * -25}
          />
          <line
            x1="0"
            y1="70%"
            x2="100%"
            y2="70%"
            stroke="url(#gradient2)"
            strokeWidth="1"
            strokeDasharray="10,15"
            strokeDashoffset={animationProgress * -25}
          />
          <line
            x1="30%"
            y1="0"
            x2="30%"
            y2="100%"
            stroke="url(#gradient3)"
            strokeWidth="1"
            strokeDasharray="10,15"
            strokeDashoffset={animationProgress * 25}
          />
          <line
            x1="70%"
            y1="0"
            x2="70%"
            y2="100%"
            stroke="url(#gradient1)"
            strokeWidth="1"
            strokeDasharray="10,15"
            strokeDashoffset={animationProgress * 25}
          />
        </svg>
      </div>

      <div className="relative z-10 flex h-full flex-col items-center justify-center">
        <div className="container mx-auto px-4">
          <motion.h2
            className="mb-16 text-center text-4xl font-bold text-white md:text-5xl lg:text-6xl"
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.8 }}
          >
            <span className="font-mono">Who Is </span>
            <span className="bg-gradient-to-r from-emerald-400 via-cyan-400 to-violet-400 bg-clip-text text-transparent">
              VoxHead
            </span>
            <span className="font-mono"> For?</span>
          </motion.h2>

          <div className="grid gap-8 md:grid-cols-12">
            {/* Category selector - clean, minimal design */}
            <div className="md:col-span-4">
              <div className="space-y-3">
                {categories.map((category, index) => (
                  <motion.button
                    key={category.id}
                    className={`group flex w-full items-center gap-4 rounded-lg border p-4 text-left transition-all duration-300 ${
                      activeIndex === index
                        ? `${category.borderColor} bg-gray-900`
                        : "border-gray-800 bg-gray-900/50 hover:border-gray-700"
                    }`}
                    onClick={() => setActiveIndex(index)}
                    initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
                    animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                    transition={{ duration: 0.5, delay: index * 0.1 }}
                  >
                    <div
                      className={`flex h-12 w-12 items-center justify-center rounded-lg ${
                        activeIndex === index ? category.bgColor : "bg-gray-800"
                      }`}
                    >
                      {category.icon}
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <h3 className={`text-lg font-medium ${activeIndex === index ? "text-white" : "text-gray-400"}`}>
                        {category.title}
                      </h3>
                      {activeIndex === index && (
                        <div
                          className="mt-1 h-0.5 w-12 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent to-transparent"
                          style={{ backgroundColor: category.color }}
                        ></div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </motion.button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Content display - clean, minimal design */}
            <div className="md:col-span-8">
              <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
                <motion.div
                  key={activeIndex}
                  className="overflow-hidden rounded-lg border border-gray-800 bg-gray-900"
                  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                  exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
                  transition={{ duration: 0.5 }}
                >
                  <div className="grid gap-6 p-6 md:grid-cols-2">
                    <div className="space-y-6">
                      <div>
                        <h3 className={`text-2xl font-bold ${categories[activeIndex].textColor}`}>
                          {categories[activeIndex].title}
                        </h3>
                        <div
                          className="mt-2 h-0.5 w-16 rounded-full"
                          style={{ backgroundColor: categories[activeIndex].color }}
                        ></div>
                      </div>

                      <p className="text-gray-300">{categories[activeIndex].description}</p>

                      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                        {categories[activeIndex].keywords.map((keyword, i) => (
                          <span
                            key={i}
                            className={`rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-sm ${categories[activeIndex].borderColor} bg-gray-900`}
                          >
                            {keyword}
                          </span>
                        ))}
                      </div>

                      <Button
                        className="mt-4 gap-2"
                        style={{ backgroundColor: categories[activeIndex].color, color: "#000" }}
                      >
                        Learn More <ArrowRight className="h-4 w-4" />
                      </Button>
                    </div>

                    <div className="flex items-center justify-center">
                      {activeIndex === 1 ? (
                        <div className="relative h-64 w-64">
                          <div
                            className="absolute inset-0 rounded-full"
                            style={{ backgroundColor: `${categories[activeIndex].color}10` }}
                          ></div>
                          <Image src="/robot-head.png" alt="VoxHead Robot" fill className="object-contain" />

                          {/* Subtle scanning effect */}
                          <div className="absolute inset-0 overflow-hidden rounded-full">
                            <div
                              className="absolute h-full w-full bg-gradient-to-b from-transparent via-cyan-500/10 to-transparent"
                              style={{
                                animation: "minimalScan 4s ease-in-out infinite",
                                top: "-100%",
                              }}
                            ></div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <div className="relative flex h-64 w-64 items-center justify-center">
                          {/* Circular progress */}
                          <svg className="absolute h-full w-full -rotate-90">
                            <circle
                              cx="50%"
                              cy="50%"
                              r="30%"
                              fill="none"
                              stroke={categories[activeIndex].color}
                              strokeWidth="1"
                              strokeDasharray="188.5"
                              strokeDashoffset="0"
                              className="opacity-10"
                            />
                            <circle
                              cx="50%"
                              cy="50%"
                              r="30%"
                              fill="none"
                              stroke={categories[activeIndex].color}
                              strokeWidth="1"
                              strokeDasharray="188.5"
                              strokeDashoffset={188.5 * (1 - animationProgress)}
                              className="opacity-50"
                            />
                          </svg>

                          <div
                            className="rounded-full p-6"
                            style={{ backgroundColor: `${categories[activeIndex].color}20` }}
                          >
                            <motion.div
                              className="text-white"
                              animate={{
                                scale: [1, 1.05, 1],
                              }}
                              transition={{
                                duration: 4,
                                repeat: Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY,
                                ease: "easeInOut",
                              }}
                            >
                              {categories[activeIndex].icon}
                            </motion.div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </motion.div>
              </AnimatePresence>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <style jsx global>{`
        @keyframes minimalScan {
          0%, 100% {
            top: -100%;
            opacity: 0;
          }
          50% {
            top: 100%;
            opacity: 0.5;
          }
        }
      `}</style>
    </section>
  )
}
================================================================================

# PRD

### **Product Requirements Document (PRD)**  
**Project Name**: Collaborative Idea Management System  
**Version**: 1.0  
**Date**: [Insert Date]  

---

### **1. Executive Summary**

The Collaborative Idea Management System is a digital platform designed to foster innovation and collaboration within the organization. It enables team members to submit, vote on, and refine ideas in a structured manner. The system prioritizes team engagement over traditional ROI metrics, with features such as nested idea creation, voting, commenting, and segmentation into internal and external categories. This PRD outlines the goals, features, user stories, technical requirements, and success metrics for the project.

---

### **2. Goals and Objectives**

#### **Primary Goal**
To create a centralized platform that empowers team members to collaboratively develop and prioritize ideas, fostering innovation and improving both internal workflows and external initiatives.

#### **Key Objectives**
1. Enable seamless submission and refinement of ideas through nested structures.
2. Facilitate team engagement via voting, commenting, and collaboration tools.
3. Segment ideas into **Internal** (workflows, processes) and **External** (initiatives, partnerships) categories for better focus.
4. Provide actionable insights through a dashboard that tracks top ideas, trends, and user activity.

---

### **3. Target Audience**

- **Primary Users**: Team members who will submit, vote on, and refine ideas.
- **Secondary Users**: Admins and managers who will monitor activity, approve ideas, and generate reports.
- **Optional Users**: External stakeholders (e.g., partners or clients) who may contribute to specific ideas.

---

### **4. Key Features**

#### **Core Features**
1. **Idea Submission**
   - Users can submit new ideas with a title, description, category (Internal/External), tags, and visibility settings.
   - Ideas are timestamped and attributed to the submitter.

2. **Nested Ideas and Comments**
   - Users can add sub-ideas or notes under existing ideas, creating a hierarchical structure.
   - Sub-ideas can also be voted on and commented on independently.

3. **Voting System**
   - Users can upvote or downvote ideas to indicate support or interest.
   - Voting scores determine the priority of ideas in each category.

4. **Commenting and Collaboration**
   - Users can leave comments on ideas and sub-ideas to provide feedback or suggestions.
   - Notifications alert users when their ideas receive votes or comments.

5. **Segmentation**
   - Ideas are categorized into:
     - **Internal**: Focus on improving workflows, processes, and tools.
     - **External**: Focus on new initiatives, partnerships, and market expansion.

6. **Dashboard and Insights**
   - A centralized dashboard displays:
     - Top-voted ideas in each category.
     - Recent activity (new submissions, comments, votes).
     - Trends in team engagement (e.g., popular topics, active users).
   - Admins can filter and export data for further analysis.

7. **Search and Filtering**
   - Users can search for ideas by keyword, category, tags, or author.
   - Advanced filters allow sorting by votes, date, or status.

8. **User Roles and Permissions**
   - **Admins**: Manage categories, approve/disapprove ideas, and monitor activity.
   - **Team Members**: Submit ideas, vote, comment, and collaborate.
   - **Guests (Optional)**: Limited access for external stakeholders.

#### **Optional Features**
1. **Gamification**
   - Badges or leaderboards to recognize top contributors.
2. **Real-Time Updates**
   - Live notifications for votes, comments, and idea updates.
3. **Integration with Tools**
   - Integration with Slack, Jira, or other collaboration tools for seamless workflows.

---

### **5. User Stories**

#### **As a Team Member**
1. **Submit an Idea**
   - "As a team member, I want to submit a new idea so that others can see it and provide feedback."
2. **Vote on an Idea**
   - "As a team member, I want to upvote or downvote an idea to show my level of support."
3. **Add a Sub-Idea**
   - "As a team member, I want to add a sub-idea under an existing idea to refine or expand on it."
4. **Leave a Comment**
   - "As a team member, I want to leave a comment on an idea to ask questions or provide suggestions."
5. **Track My Contributions**
   - "As a team member, I want to see all the ideas I’ve submitted, voted on, or commented on in one place."

#### **As an Admin**
1. **Monitor Activity**
   - "As an admin, I want to view a dashboard of recent activity and top ideas to stay informed."
2. **Approve/Disapprove Ideas**
   - "As an admin, I want to approve or disapprove ideas to ensure they align with organizational goals."
3. **Generate Reports**
   - "As an admin, I want to export data on idea submissions, votes, and engagement for analysis."

---

### **6. Technical Requirements**

#### **Frontend**
- **Framework**: React.js or Vue.js for a responsive and interactive UI.
- **Components**:
  - Idea submission form.
  - Nested idea/comment threads.
  - Voting buttons and score displays.
  - Dashboard visualizations (charts, lists).

#### **Backend**
- **Framework**: Node.js with Express.js or Django for backend logic.
- **Database**:
  - Relational database (PostgreSQL/MySQL) for structured data.
  - NoSQL database (MongoDB) for unstructured data (optional).
- **API**:
  - RESTful APIs for CRUD operations on ideas, votes, and comments.
  - WebSocket or similar technology for real-time updates.

#### **Authentication**
- Use OAuth 2.0 or JWT for secure user authentication.
- Role-based access control (RBAC) for permissions.

#### **Hosting**
- Cloud platforms like AWS, Azure, or Google Cloud.
- Docker for containerization and Kubernetes for orchestration.

---

### **7. Success Metrics**

1. **User Engagement**
   - Number of active users submitting, voting, or commenting on ideas.
   - Average time spent on the platform per user.

2. **Idea Adoption**
   - Percentage of ideas marked as "In Progress" or "Completed."
   - Number of sub-ideas created under top-level ideas.

3. **Collaboration**
   - Average number of comments per idea.
   - Frequency of cross-team collaboration on ideas.

4. **Dashboard Usage**
   - Number of times the dashboard is accessed by admins.
   - Insights generated from exported reports.

5. **Gamification (if implemented)**
   - Number of badges earned or leaderboard positions achieved.

---

### **8. Development Phases**

#### **Phase 1: Core Functionality**
- Build basic idea submission, voting, and commenting.
- Implement segmentation into Internal and External categories.

#### **Phase 2: Nested Ideas and Collaboration**
- Add support for nested ideas and sub-comments.
- Enhance the commenting system with @mentions and notifications.

#### **Phase 3: Dashboard and Analytics**
- Develop a dashboard for tracking top ideas, recent activity, and engagement trends.
- Include exportable reports for admins.

#### **Phase 4: Gamification and Advanced Features**
- Introduce badges, leaderboards, and rewards for active contributors.
- Add advanced filtering and search capabilities.

---

### **9. Risks and Mitigation**

| Risk                          | Mitigation Strategy                                     |
|-------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------|
| Low user adoption             | Conduct workshops and training sessions to onboard users. |
| Data overload                 | Implement robust filtering and search features.        |
| Security breaches             | Use OAuth 2.0/JWT and follow best practices for data security. |
| Real-time performance issues  | Optimize API calls and use caching where necessary.    |

---

### **10. Timeline**

| Phase                  | Estimated Duration | Start Date | End Date   |
|------------------------|--------------------|------------|------------|
| Core Functionality     | 2 months          | [Insert]   | [Insert]   |
| Nested Ideas           | 1 month           | [Insert]   | [Insert]   |
| Dashboard and Analytics| 1.5 months        | [Insert]   | [Insert]   |
| Gamification           | 1 month           | [Insert]   | [Insert]   |

---

### **11. Conclusion**

The Collaborative Idea Management System will empower your organization to harness collective creativity and drive meaningful change. By focusing on team engagement, collaboration, and transparency, this platform will become a cornerstone of innovation within your organization. Let me know if you'd like to refine any section or proceed to the next steps!

[ ] Stakeholders
